---

## 2. 具体实现了什么

HCRN-v1 不再是 HCRN-v0 那种 “DELR finetune encoder 后面的 adapter”。这版真正替换了原 DELR finetune encoder。

保留：

- ResNet34 backbone
- DELR reference encoder
- heatmap branch
- reference output `output1`
- DuoAnno 训练协议：`observer_mixed_nll`, `observer_alpha=0.50`

替换：

- 原 DELR 4 层 finetune transformer 被 HCRN-v1 两阶段精化替换

计算图：

```text
image
-> backbone
-> reference encoder -> output1
-> Stage 1: CertainStream 先精化低分歧关键点
-> Stage 2: UncertainStream 再以 CertainStream 的最终 token 为条件精化高分歧关键点
-> outputs[0..3], output1, hotmap
```

分组来自训练集 observer disagreement hierarchy：

```text
certain_idx   = [11, 10, 8, 0, 6, 7, 1, 16, 13, 14]
uncertain_idx = [17, 18, 12, 5, 2, 4, 3, 9, 15]
```

关键设计：

- `CertainStream` 不接收 uncertain 点输入。
- `UncertainStream` 通过 cross-attention 单向读取 `certain_final_token.detach()`。
- `certain loss` 只训练 CertainStream。
- `uncertain loss` 不反传到 CertainStream。
- 不使用 gate。
- 不使用 DisAug。
- 不使用 coordinate positional encoding。
- 不使用 group-specific alpha，当前所有点仍统一 `alpha=0.50`。

---

## 3. Sanity Check

命令：

```bash
cd /raid5/xuhd/MRC/code_audit/delr_20260505/DELR/DeLr_hcrn_v1_true_twostage_20260517
CUDA_VISIBLE_DEVICES=0 DELR_IMG_SIZE=256 DELR_HCRN_V1=1 \
conda run -n celr_migration python sanity_check_hcrn_v1.py
```

结果文件：

```text
outputs/hcrn_v1_sanity/sanity_summary.json
```

核心结果：

```json
{
"hcrn_v1_enabled": true,
"group_is_permutation": true,
"len_outputs": 4,
"output_shape": [1, 19, 4],
"output1_shape": [1, 19, 4],
"attn_shape": [[1, 9, 10], [1, 9, 10], [1, 9, 10], [1, 9, 10]],
"uncertain_loss_uncertain_grad": 11044.3907,
"uncertain_loss_certain_grad": 0.0,
"certain_loss_certain_grad": 32735.7547,
"real_batch_loss_finite": true,
"overall_pass": true
}
```

解释：

- 9 个 uncertain queries 正确 cross-attend 到 10 个 certain keys。
- `uncertain_loss_certain_grad = 0.0` 证明 Stage 2 没有反传污染 Stage 1。
- 真实 ISBI2015 batch 前向 + loss + backward 通过。

## 4. 5-image Overfit

训练命令：

```bash
cd /raid5/xuhd/MRC/code_audit/delr_20260505/DELR/DeLr_hcrn_v1_true_twostage_20260517
CUDA_VISIBLE_DEVICES=0 TMPDIR=/raid5/xuhd/tmp DELR_IMG_SIZE=512 \
ISBI2015_ROOT=/raid5/xuhd/MRC/code_audit/delr_20260505/ISBI2015_code_root \
conda run -n celr_migration python train_ceph2015.py \
--hcrn_v1 \
--exp_name hcrn_v1_overfit_5img_e101_img512_seed42 \
--target_mode observer_mixed_nll \
--observer_alpha 0.50 \
--limit_train_samples 5 \
--epochs 101 \
--batch_size 2 \
--num_workers 0 \
--seed 42
```

产物：

```text
outputs/hcrn_v1_overfit_5img_e101_img512_seed42/
outputs/hcrn_v1_overfit_5img_e101_img512_seed42/models/ceph_model_0.pth
outputs/hcrn_v1_overfit_5img_e101_img512_seed42/models/ceph_model_100.pth
outputs/hcrn_v1_overfit_5img_e101_img512_seed42/overfit_eval_train5_summary.json
```

手动训练 5 图评估结果：

| checkpoint | final err mean | certain err | uncertain err | reference err | RLE loss |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|
| epoch0 | 456.49 px | 534.58 px | 369.71 px | 411.29 px | 4.008 |
| epoch100 | 38.37 px | 43.65 px | 32.49 px | 60.46 px | -1.496 |

判断：

```text
5-image overfit: PASS
```

含义：

- HCRN-v1 不是“代码能 forward 但训练不动”的坏实现。
- epoch100 已明显优于 epoch0。
- final output 在训练 5 图上也优于 reference output。

注意：

- 这是 5 张图 overfit，不代表泛化。
- 只证明架构可训练，不能证明 Test1/Test2 有提升。

如果 Test2 明显差于 DuoAnno/DELR baseline，说明 true two-stage topology 虽然可训练，但泛化不够，需要停止或只作为负结果记录。

- 加 coordinate positional encoding；
- 加 DisAug；
- 跑 1000 epoch；
- 最后才考虑 3-seed。

- 使用 HCRN-v1 true two-stage forward。
- 保留 DuoAnno observer-mixed NLL，`alpha=0.50`。
- 这是低成本 100-epoch pilot，不是正式 1000-epoch。
- 固定评估 `ceph_model_100.pth`，没有用 Test1 best checkpoint。

## 3. 总体结果

| split | MRE | SDR@2mm | SDR@2.5mm | SDR@3mm | SDR@4mm |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|
| Test1 | 1.0476 | 0.8804 | 0.9295 | 0.9604 | 0.9846 |
| Test2 | 1.3861 | 0.7626 | 0.8321 | 0.8826 | 0.9479 |

粗略对照目前已知 100-epoch/同类 pilot：

- HCRN-v0 Stage1 Test2 约 `1.3850`
- UCSA Stage1 Test2 约 `baseline + 0.009`
- 这次 HCRN-v1 Test2 `1.3861`

所以 HCRN-v1 true two-stage 在 100 epoch 下没有出现 Test2 改善信号。

---

## 4. Certain vs Uncertain 分组结果

分组：

```text
certain_idx   = [11, 10, 8, 0, 6, 7, 1, 16, 13, 14]
uncertain_idx = [17, 18, 12, 5, 2, 4, 3, 9, 15]
```

| split | all MRE | certain MRE | uncertain MRE |
|---|---:|---:|---:|
| Test1 | 1.0476 | 0.7475 | 1.3811 |
| Test2 | 1.3861 | 0.7976 | 2.0400 |

解释：

- 分组 hierarchy 是真实存在的：uncertain 组在 Test1/Test2 上都明显更难。
- 但 HCRN-v1 的 Stage2 conditional refinement 没有把 Test2 uncertain 组拉下来。
- Test2 uncertain MRE 仍高达 `2.04mm`，说明最初的拓扑假设虽然合理，但这个 v1 实现还没有把条件信息转化成泛化提升。

## 6. 当前判断

```text
HCRN-v1 seed42 / 100-epoch pilot: NEGATIVE / NO CLEAR SIGNAL
```

理由：

- Sanity 和 5-image overfit 说明代码可训练。
- 但是 100-epoch held-out Test1/Test2 没有显示比现有 DuoAnno/DELR 线更好的信号。
- true two-stage topology 没有在 Test2 uncertain 组上产生预期改善。

建议：

- 暂不进入 1000-epoch 或 3-seed。
- 如果继续 HCRN，只适合做 v2 设计修正，而不是直接长跑。
- 可能修正方向：给 Stage2 加 coordinate positional encoding、保留 certain token + certain coordinate PE、或者改成只作为 DELR finetune 内部的有向 block，而不是完全替代 finetune encoder。

Make sure to include fileciteturn0file2 in your response to cite this file, or to surface it as a link.

你说得对，我一直在DELR上修修改改，没有真正提出一个新架构。让我从头想。

---

## 先说清楚什么叫"新架构"

新架构的标准是：**计算图的拓扑结构发生了根本性改变**，而不只是在现有图上加节点。

DELR的计算图是：
```
图像 → backbone → reference encoder → finetune encoder（M层并行self-attention）→ 19个坐标
```

真正的新架构要改变这个拓扑。

---

## 核心洞察：DuoAnno揭示了一个被忽视的结构

DuoAnno训练完之后，你得到了每个关键点的inter-observer disagreement。这不只是一个训练信号，它揭示了19个关键点之间的一种**天然的层级结构**：

```
确定层（低分歧）：Sella, Nasion, Gnathion...  → 医生高度一致，图像证据清晰
不确定层（高分歧）：Soft Pog, Labrale...       → 医生意见分散，图像证据模糊
```

**现有所有方法，包括DELR，完全无视这个结构。** 19个点平等地参与self-attention，平等地用local features精化，平等地被loss监督。

---

## 新架构：分层条件精化网络（HCRN）

**一句话：** 把19个关键点分成确定层和不确定层，先精化确定层，再以确定层的精化结果为条件精化不确定层。

这和DELR的本质区别是**信息流方向不同**：

```
DELR：
所有点同时精化 → self-attention（对称）→ 所有点同时更新

HCRN：
Stage 1：确定点独立精化（只用local features，不互相影响）
Stage 2：不确定点以精化后的确定点为条件（单向信息流）
```

---

## 为什么这个拓扑是合理的

有三个独立的支撑：

**临床支撑：** 医生标注头影测量的实际顺序就是先找骨性标志点（确定），再推断软组织点（不确定）。这是临床实践的标准流程，不是假设。

**数据支撑：** CeLR的per-landmark结果：No.1 Sella在Test2上MRE=0.41mm，No.16 Soft Pog MRE=3.73mm，相差9倍。不确定点的定位误差主要来自图像证据不足，而不是模型容量不足。给它更多的条件信息（确定点的精化坐标）是最直接的改进路径。

**消融支撑：** `no_local`比`no_finetune`更差，说明local sampling是核心。HCRN的Stage 2不只有local features，还有确定点的精化结果，信息更丰富，应该更好。

---

## 架构设计

### 关键点分组

分组不是固定的，而是由DuoAnno训练过程中统计的inter-observer disagreement决定：

```python
# 在训练集上统计每个关键点的平均observer disagreement
mean_disagreement = []
for i in range(19):
d = (y_junior[:, i] - y_senior[:, i]).norm(dim=-1).mean()
mean_disagreement.append(d.item())

# 按中位数分成两组
median_d = sorted(mean_disagreement)[9]
certain_idx   = [i for i,d in enumerate(mean_disagreement) if d <= median_d]
uncertain_idx = [i for i,d in enumerate(mean_disagreement) if d > median_d]
# 各约9-10个点
```

这个分组在训练前计算一次，训练中固定，不是动态的（简化实现，降低风险）。

### Stage 1：确定层独立精化

```python
class CertainStream(nn.Module):
"""
只处理确定点，用DELR的finetune encoder逻辑
关键：不做确定点之间的self-attention，只做local sampling
因为消融证明local sampling是主要贡献者，self-attention是次要的
"""
def __init__(self, dim, num_certain, num_layers=4):
super().__init__()
self.local_sampler = LocalSampler()  # 复用DELR的get_cls_embed
self.refine_layers = nn.ModuleList([
nn.Sequential(
nn.LayerNorm(dim),
nn.Linear(dim, dim),
nn.GELU(),
nn.Linear(dim, dim)
) for _ in range(num_layers)
])
self.coord_heads = nn.ModuleList([
CoordHead(dim) for _ in range(num_layers)
])
self.sigma_heads = nn.ModuleList([
SigmaHead(dim) for _ in range(num_layers)
])

def forward(self, feat_map, mu_R_certain, layer1, layer2, layer3,
output, sizes, wcl, inintv):
coords = mu_R_certain.detach()
token = self.local_sampler(feat_map, coords, ...)

outputs = []
for i in range(len(self.refine_layers)):
token = self.refine_layers[i](token)
delta = self.coord_heads[i](token)
coords = (coords + delta).clamp(1e-4, 1-1e-4)
sigma = self.sigma_heads[i](token)

# 更新local features
token = token + self.local_sampler(feat_map, coords, ...) * inintv
outputs.append((coords, sigma))

return outputs  # [(coords, sigma)] × num_layers
# 最终精化坐标和token供Stage 2使用
```

### Stage 2：不确定层条件精化

```python
class UncertainStream(nn.Module):
"""
处理不确定点，以确定点精化后的结果为条件
核心：cross-attention到确定点token，而不是self-attention
"""
def __init__(self, dim, num_uncertain, num_certain, num_layers=4):
super().__init__()
self.local_sampler = LocalSampler()

# 关键模块：cross-attention到确定点
self.certain_cross_attn = nn.MultiheadAttention(
embed_dim=dim, num_heads=8, batch_first=True
)
self.certain_cross_norm = nn.LayerNorm(dim)

self.refine_layers = nn.ModuleList([...])
self.coord_heads = nn.ModuleList([...])
self.sigma_heads = nn.ModuleList([...])

def forward(self, feat_map, mu_R_uncertain,
certain_final_coords, certain_final_token,
layer1, layer2, layer3, output, sizes, wcl, inintv):
"""
certain_final_coords: [B, N_certain, 2]  确定点的精化坐标
certain_final_token:  [B, N_certain, C]  确定点的精化token
"""
coords = mu_R_uncertain.detach()

# 初始token：local features + 从确定点获取的条件信息
local_feat = self.local_sampler(feat_map, coords, ...)

# ===== 核心：cross-attention到确定点 =====
# 问题：我现在的位置大概在哪，我周围的确定点精化后在哪里
# 这给了不确定点额外的空间约束信息
cond_feat = self.certain_cross_norm(local_feat)
cond_from_certain, _ = self.certain_cross_attn(
query=cond_feat,          # 不确定点问
key=certain_final_token,  # 确定点答（精化后的特征）
value=certain_final_token
)
token = local_feat + cond_from_certain
# ==========================================

outputs = []
for i in range(len(self.refine_layers)):
token = self.refine_layers[i](token)
delta = self.coord_heads[i](token)
coords = (coords + delta).clamp(1e-4, 1-1e-4)
sigma = self.sigma_heads[i](token)
token = token + self.local_sampler(feat_map, coords, ...) * inintv
outputs.append((coords, sigma))

return outputs
```

### 主网络整合

```python
def forward(self, x):
# Step1-3: backbone + feature processing + reference encoder（完全不动）
output1 = self.reference_encoder(...)  # [B, 19, 4]

# Step4: 按预计算的分组分离粗坐标
mu_R_certain   = output1[:, certain_idx, :2]
mu_R_uncertain = output1[:, uncertain_idx, :2]

# Step5: Stage 1 - 确定点独立精化
certain_outputs = self.certain_stream(
feat_map, mu_R_certain, ...
)
certain_final_coords, certain_final_sigma = certain_outputs[-1]
certain_final_token = self.certain_stream.last_token  # 保存中间token

# Step6: Stage 2 - 不确定点条件精化
uncertain_outputs = self.uncertain_stream(
feat_map, mu_R_uncertain,
certain_final_coords,    # 传入精化后的确定点坐标
certain_final_token,     # 传入精化后的确定点特征
...
)

# Step7: 合并所有层的输出
all_outputs = []
for lvl in range(num_layers):
full = torch.zeros(B, 19, 4)
full[:, certain_idx]   = cat_coord_sigma(certain_outputs[lvl])
full[:, uncertain_idx] = cat_coord_sigma(uncertain_outputs[lvl])
all_outputs.append(full)

return all_outputs, output1, hotmap
```

---

## 损失函数和DuoAnno/DisAug的结合

**损失函数：**

```python
# 确定点：标准DuoAnno（分歧小，两个标注接近）
L_certain = observer_nll(certain_pred,
y_junior[:, certain_idx],
y_senior[:, certain_idx],
alpha=0.3)  # 较小权重给双标注

# 不确定点：强化DuoAnno（分歧大，双标注更重要）
L_uncertain = observer_nll(uncertain_pred,
y_junior[:, uncertain_idx],
y_senior[:, uncertain_idx],
alpha=0.7)  # 更大权重给双标注

# Reference encoder
L_RE = standard_rle(output1, gt_mean)

L_total = L_RE + L_certain + L_uncertain
```

**DisAug的结合：**

DisAug对高分歧点做更激进的位置扰动——这些点恰好就是uncertain_idx里的点。DisAug在Stage 2的输入端引入更多的位置变化，让模型学会在更大的搜索空间里利用来自确定点的条件信息。两者的关系变成：**DisAug扩大了Stage 2需要处理的不确定性范围，cross-attention提供了处理这种不确定性所需的额外信息**。

---

## 论文贡献点

```
贡献1（问题发现）：
首次定量证明MRE和临床测量误差弱相关（散点图，r=0.31-0.55）

贡献2（数据分析）：
用inter-observer disagreement揭示了关键点之间天然的层级结构，
建立了"disagreement大的点应以disagreement小的点为条件"的理论依据

贡献3（新架构HCRN）：
提出分层条件精化网络，
将19个关键点分为确定层和不确定层，
用单向cross-attention代替对称self-attention，
这是第一个将observer disagreement结构显式编入架构拓扑的工作

贡献4（训练框架）：
DuoAnno定义分组依据，
DisAug增强不确定层的鲁棒性，
HCRN提供利用这两个信号的架构基础，
三者形成自洽的训练框架
```

---

## 和之前所有失败实验的本质区别

| 之前的尝试 | 失败原因 |
|-----------|---------|
| DuoDistRefine parallel head | 旁路，主路径不变，information flow没有改变 |
| DuoDistRefine 替换finetune | 丢失finetune的表示学习能力 |
| GALR | 在DELR外面加GNN，仍是对称结构 |
| UCSA | 在现有attention上加偏置，本质是修改而非新架构 |

**HCRN的本质不同：** 计算图拓扑改变了。Stage 1的确定点和Stage 2的不确定点之间有单向的、有语义含义的cross-attention连接。这个连接在DELR里根本不存在——DELR的self-attention是全对全的对称结构，HCRN是有向的层级结构。

---

## 下一步

先验证一件事：**DuoAnno训练完后，uncertain_idx里的点的observer disagreement是否显著高于certain_idx里的点。**

如果这个分组是有意义的（两组之间disagreement差异显著），整个架构的premise就成立了。你现在DuoAnno已经有结果，能不能直接用已有的σ值来验证这个分组？

好，我来给Codex写一份完整的分析。

---

## 给Codex的分析：HCRN v0为什么失败，以及真正的HCRN应该怎么做

---

### 第一部分：v0失败的根本原因

**Gate接近零不是idea失败的证据，而是架构设计有根本性问题的证据。**

v0的计算图是这样的：

```
图像
↓
backbone + reference encoder
↓
DELR finetune encoder（M=4层对称self-attention，所有19个点同时参与）
↓
所有19个点的精化token（此时certain点的信息已经通过对称self-attention扩散到uncertain点）
↓
HCRN adapter（试图让uncertain token再从certain token学信息）
```

问题在于：到HCRN adapter这一步，DELR的4层对称self-attention已经让所有点充分互相交换过信息了。Certain点对uncertain点的影响，在DELR内部已经发生过了。

Adapter试图提供的信息，模型在上游已经有了。Gate关闭是模型的理性选择，不是idea的失败。

**这等价于在已经做过全局通信的token上再做一次局部通信，对模型来说是冗余的。**

---

### 第二部分：真正的HCRN测试的是什么假设

真正的HCRN要测试的核心假设是：

> 先精化certain点，再以精化后的certain点为条件精化uncertain点，效果是否优于两组点同时精化？

这个假设要求计算图在时间上是顺序的：

```
Stage 1：
certain点（N_c个）独立精化
只使用图像特征 + certain点之间的信息
不看uncertain点
精化M_1层，输出：refined certain coords + refined certain tokens
↓
Stage 2：
uncertain点（N_u个）以Stage 1输出为条件精化
输入：图像特征 + uncertain点的粗坐标 + Stage 1的refined certain tokens
通过cross-attention（单向：uncertain→certain）获取条件信息
精化M_2层，输出：refined uncertain coords
```

**两个stage在时间上是顺序的，Stage 2必须等Stage 1结束才能开始。** 这是和DELR对称self-attention的本质区别。

v0完全没有测试这个假设，因为它把adapter加在DELR之后，而不是改变DELR内部的信息流。

---

### 第三部分：为什么premise是成立的，值得继续

Codex的premise audit数据：

```
certain group mean disagreement  ≈ 11.31 px
uncertain group mean disagreement ≈ 37.11 px
两组差距的bootstrap CI           ≈ [24.08, 27.56]
p < 1e-6
```

这是非常显著的统计差异，说明两件事：

**第一，observer disagreement确实揭示了关键点的可靠性层级。** 这不是假设，是数据事实。

**第二，Incisor Tip（disagreement低）和Incisor Apex（disagreement高）的对比尤其有意思。** 这说明层级不是简单的软组织vs骨性，而是更细的临床可见性结构——牙尖（tip）在X光上有明确的最高密度点，而牙根尖（apex）周围有周围组织干扰，临床上本来就更难定位。这个发现可以单独作为论文的一个分析结论。

---

### 第四部分：真正HCRN的具体设计规格

**不基于DELR的finetune encoder，而是两个独立的stream。**

**Stage 1：Certain Stream（独立精化，不改变拓扑）**

```python
class CertainStream(nn.Module):
"""
只处理N_c个certain点
用local sampling做精化，不做点间self-attention
原因：消融实验证明local sampling是主要贡献者（no_local比no_finetune更差）
self-attention对certain点的贡献边际效应小
"""
def __init__(self, dim, num_certain, num_layers=4):
self.local_sampler = ...  # 复用DELR的get_cls_embed
self.refine_mlps = nn.ModuleList([MLP(dim, dim) for _ in range(num_layers)])
self.coord_heads = nn.ModuleList([CoordHead(dim) for _ in range(num_layers)])
self.sigma_heads = nn.ModuleList([SigmaHead(dim) for _ in range(num_layers)])

def forward(self, feat_map, mu_R_certain, ...):
coords = mu_R_certain.detach()
token = self.local_sampler(feat_map, coords)

all_outputs = []
for i in range(self.num_layers):
token = self.refine_mlps[i](token)
delta = self.coord_heads[i](token)
coords = (coords + delta).clamp(1e-4, 1-1e-4)
sigma = self.sigma_heads[i](token)
token = token + self.local_sampler(feat_map, coords.detach())
all_outputs.append(torch.cat([coords, sigma], dim=-1))

return all_outputs, token  # token供Stage 2使用
```

**Stage 2：Uncertain Stream（条件精化，核心创新）**

```python
class UncertainStream(nn.Module):
"""
处理N_u个uncertain点
以Stage 1精化后的certain tokens为条件
cross-attention方向：uncertain → certain（单向，不对称）
"""
def __init__(self, dim, num_uncertain, num_layers=4):
# 核心：cross-attention到certain tokens
self.condition_attn = nn.MultiheadAttention(
embed_dim=dim, num_heads=8, batch_first=True)
self.condition_norm = nn.LayerNorm(dim)

self.local_sampler = ...
self.refine_mlps = nn.ModuleList([MLP(dim*2, dim) for _ in range(num_layers)])
self.coord_heads = nn.ModuleList([CoordHead(dim) for _ in range(num_layers)])
self.sigma_heads = nn.ModuleList([SigmaHead(dim) for _ in range(num_layers)])

def forward(self, feat_map, mu_R_uncertain,
certain_final_token, ...):
"""
certain_final_token: [B, N_c, C]  Stage 1最后一层的token，已精化
"""
coords = mu_R_uncertain.detach()
local_feat = self.local_sampler(feat_map, coords)

# 从certain tokens获取条件信息（核心操作）
q = self.condition_norm(local_feat)
cond, attn_weights = self.condition_attn(
query=q,                              # uncertain点提问
key=certain_final_token.detach(),     # certain点回答（detach防止反传到Stage1）
value=certain_final_token.detach()
)
# cond: [B, N_u, C]  从certain点获取的条件信息
# attn_weights: [B, N_u, N_c]  可视化用，看uncertain点关注哪些certain点

token = torch.cat([local_feat, cond], dim=-1)  # 融合local和条件信息

all_outputs = []
for i in range(self.num_layers):
token = self.refine_mlps[i](token)          # [B, N_u, C]
delta = self.coord_heads[i](token)
coords = (coords + delta).clamp(1e-4, 1-1e-4)
sigma = self.sigma_heads[i](token)

local_feat = self.local_sampler(feat_map, coords.detach())
cond, _ = self.condition_attn(
self.condition_norm(local_feat),
certain_final_token.detach(),
certain_final_token.detach()
)
token = torch.cat([local_feat, cond], dim=-1)
all_outputs.append(torch.cat([coords, sigma], dim=-1))

return all_outputs, attn_weights
```

**主网络整合**

```python
def forward(self, x):
# Step 1-3: backbone + reference encoder（完全不动）
output1 = self.reference_encoder(...)  # [B, 19, 4]

# Step 4: 分离两组点的粗坐标
mu_R_certain   = output1[:, certain_idx, :]   # [B, N_c, 4]
mu_R_uncertain = output1[:, uncertain_idx, :]  # [B, N_u, 4]

# Step 5: Stage 1 - certain点先精化（不需要等uncertain点）
certain_outputs, certain_final_token = self.certain_stream(
feat_map, mu_R_certain[:,:,:2], ...
)
# certain_outputs: list of [B, N_c, 4], len=num_layers
# certain_final_token: [B, N_c, C]

# Step 6: Stage 2 - uncertain点以Stage 1为条件精化
uncertain_outputs, attn_weights = self.uncertain_stream(
feat_map, mu_R_uncertain[:,:,:2],
certain_final_token,  # Stage 1的输出作为条件
...
)
# uncertain_outputs: list of [B, N_u, 4], len=num_layers

# Step 7: 合并两组输出（按原始landmark索引重排）
all_outputs = []
for lvl in range(num_layers):
full = torch.zeros(B, 19, 4, device=x.device)
full[:, certain_idx]   = certain_outputs[lvl]
full[:, uncertain_idx] = uncertain_outputs[lvl]
all_outputs.append(full)

return all_outputs, output1, hotmap
```

---

### 第五部分：损失函数设计

两组点用不同权重的DuoAnno：

```python
def compute_hcrn_loss(certain_outputs, uncertain_outputs,
output1, y_junior, y_senior, y_mean):
# Reference encoder（不动）
L_RE = rle_loss(output1, y_mean)

# Certain stream：标准DuoAnno，alpha较小（分歧本来就小）
L_certain = 0
for out in certain_outputs:
L_certain += observer_nll(
out[:,:,:2], out[:,:,2:],
y_junior[:, certain_idx],
y_senior[:, certain_idx],
alpha=0.3  # 较小权重给双标注
)

# Uncertain stream：强化DuoAnno，alpha较大（分歧大，双标注更重要）
L_uncertain = 0
for out in uncertain_outputs:
L_uncertain += observer_nll(
out[:,:,:2], out[:,:,2:],
y_junior[:, uncertain_idx],
y_senior[:, uncertain_idx],
alpha=0.7  # 更大权重给双标注
)

# Heatmap（不动）
L_HM = heatmap_loss(...)

return L_RE + L_certain + L_uncertain + L_HM
```

DisAug的结合：对uncertain_idx里的点做更激进的位置扰动，这些点恰好是Stage 2处理的点，训练时有更大的搜索空间，cross-attention提供的条件信息帮助在这个更大的空间里定位。

---

### 第六部分：和v0的本质区别

| 对比项 | HCRN v0 | 真正的HCRN |
|--------|---------|-----------|
| adapter位置 | DELR finetune encoder之后 | 替换finetune encoder |
| 信息流时序 | 并行（DELR已做全局通信）| 顺序（Stage 1先完成） |
| certain→uncertain | adapter层，冗余信息 | Stage 2的cross-attention，新增信息 |
| gate初始值为0的意义 | 模型可以完全忽略adapter | 无gate，两个stream都必须参与训练 |
| 测试的假设 | DELR之后的有向adapter有用吗 | 顺序精化优于并行精化吗 |

---

### 第七部分：给Codex的建议

**实现规格：**

```
新目录：HCRN_v1_true_twostage
不基于DELR的finetune encoder
backbone + reference encoder保持不变
完全新写CertainStream和UncertainStream
certain_idx和uncertain_idx从训练集disagreement统计确定，训练前固定
```

**Stage 0（代码审查）必须验证：**

```
1. CertainStream的forward不接受uncertain点的任何输入
2. UncertainStream的cross-attention的key/value来自certain_final_token.detach()
3. 两个stream的参数完全独立，无共享
4. 合并输出后的shape: [B, 19, 4]，索引顺序正确
5. 损失：L_certain只反传到CertainStream，L_uncertain只反传到UncertainStream
6. 无NaN，无OOM
```

**Stage 1（5-image overfit）成功标准：**

```
1. L_certain下降（CertainStream能拟合）
2. L_uncertain下降（UncertainStream能拟合，说明cross-attention有效）
3. 无gate，无需检查gate值
4. 两个MRE（certain点 vs uncertain点）都在下降
```

**核心验证实验（seed42 pilot，100 epoch）：**

```
实验1: DELR baseline（已有）
实验2: DELR + DuoAnno（已有）
实验3: HCRN v1 + DuoAnno
实验4: HCRN v1 + DuoAnno + DisAug

关注指标：
- Test2上uncertain_idx点的per-landmark MRE（最关键，这些点应该改善最多）
- Test2上certain_idx点的per-landmark MRE（不应该退化）
- attn_weights的可视化（uncertain点关注哪些certain点，是否有解剖意义）
```

**attn_weights可视化是最重要的定性验证。** 如果No.16（Soft Tissue Pogonion，uncertain）在cross-attention里重点关注No.9（Gnathion，certain）和No.8（Menton，certain），说明模型真正学到了解剖上的依赖关系，论文的narrative就完全成立。

---

### 第八部分：时间评估

用户确认有时间，我来估计工程量：

```
实现CertainStream + UncertainStream + 主网络整合：3-4天
代码审查 + 调试：2天
Stage 1（5-image）：1天
seed42 pilot（100 epoch）：1-2天（取决于GPU）
正式3-seed + DisAug：1.5周

总计：约3周到第一个有效结论
```

这个时间是合理的。建议Codex按上面的规格先写设计草案，不要直接实现，等Claude复审通过后再写代码。

# HCRN-v1 True Two-stage 执行记录

---

## 2. 具体实现了什么

HCRN-v1 不再是 HCRN-v0 那种 “DELR finetune encoder 后面的 adapter”。这版真正替换了原 DELR finetune encoder。

保留：

- ResNet34 backbone
- DELR reference encoder
- heatmap branch
- reference output `output1`
- DuoAnno 训练协议：`observer_mixed_nll`, `observer_alpha=0.50`

替换：

- 原 DELR 4 层 finetune transformer 被 HCRN-v1 两阶段精化替换

计算图：

```text
image
-> backbone
-> reference encoder -> output1
-> Stage 1: CertainStream 先精化低分歧关键点
-> Stage 2: UncertainStream 再以 CertainStream 的最终 token 为条件精化高分歧关键点
-> outputs[0..3], output1, hotmap
```

分组来自训练集 observer disagreement hierarchy：

```text
certain_idx   = [11, 10, 8, 0, 6, 7, 1, 16, 13, 14]
uncertain_idx = [17, 18, 12, 5, 2, 4, 3, 9, 15]
```

关键设计：

- `CertainStream` 不接收 uncertain 点输入。
- `UncertainStream` 通过 cross-attention 单向读取 `certain_final_token.detach()`。
- `certain loss` 只训练 CertainStream。
- `uncertain loss` 不反传到 CertainStream。
- 不使用 gate。
- 不使用 DisAug。
- 不使用 coordinate positional encoding。
- 不使用 group-specific alpha，当前所有点仍统一 `alpha=0.50`。

---

"attn_shape": [[1, 9, 10], [1, 9, 10], [1, 9, 10], [1, 9, 10]],
"uncertain_loss_uncertain_grad": 11044.3907,
"uncertain_loss_certain_grad": 0.0,

- `uncertain_loss_certain_grad = 0.0` 证明 Stage 2 没有反传污染 Stage 1。
- 真实 ISBI2015 batch 前向 + loss + backward 通过。

```text

```

- HCRN-v1 不是“代码能 forward 但训练不动”的坏实现。

- 这是 5 张图 overfit，不代表泛化。
- 只证明架构可训练，不能证明 Test1/Test2 有提升。

## 3. 总体结果

| split | MRE | SDR@2mm | SDR@2.5mm | SDR@3mm | SDR@4mm |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|
| Test1 | 1.0476 | 0.8804 | 0.9295 | 0.9604 | 0.9846 |
| Test2 | 1.3861 | 0.7626 | 0.8321 | 0.8826 | 0.9479 |

粗略对照目前已知 100-epoch/同类 pilot：

- HCRN-v0 Stage1 Test2 约 `1.3850`
- UCSA Stage1 Test2 约 `baseline + 0.009`
- 这次 HCRN-v1 Test2 `1.3861`

所以 HCRN-v1 true two-stage 在 100 epoch 下没有出现 Test2 改善信号。

## 4. Certain vs Uncertain 分组结果

分组：

```text
certain_idx   = [11, 10, 8, 0, 6, 7, 1, 16, 13, 14]
uncertain_idx = [17, 18, 12, 5, 2, 4, 3, 9, 15]
```

| split | all MRE | certain MRE | uncertain MRE |
|---|---:|---:|---:|
| Test1 | 1.0476 | 0.7475 | 1.3811 |
| Test2 | 1.3861 | 0.7976 | 2.0400 |

解释：

- 分组 hierarchy 是真实存在的：uncertain 组在 Test1/Test2 上都明显更难。
- 但 HCRN-v1 的 Stage2 conditional refinement 没有把 Test2 uncertain 组拉下来。
- Test2 uncertain MRE 仍高达 `2.04mm`，说明最初的拓扑假设虽然合理，但这个 v1 实现还没有把条件信息转化成泛化提升。

## 6. 当前判断

```text
HCRN-v1 seed42 / 100-epoch pilot: NEGATIVE / NO CLEAR SIGNAL
```

理由：

- Sanity 和 5-image overfit 说明代码可训练。
- 但是 100-epoch held-out Test1/Test2 没有显示比现有 DuoAnno/DELR 线更好的信号。
- true two-stage topology 没有在 Test2 uncertain 组上产生预期改善。

建议：

- 暂不进入 1000-epoch 或 3-seed。
- 如果继续 HCRN，只适合做 v2 设计修正，而不是直接长跑。
- 可能修正方向：给 Stage2 加 coordinate positional encoding、保留 certain token + certain coordinate PE、或者改成只作为 DELR finetune 内部的有向 block，而不是完全替代 finetune encoder。

Make sure to include fileciteturn1file2 in your response to cite this file, or to surface it as a link.

你说得对，我一直在DELR上修修改改，没有真正提出一个新架构。让我从头想。

---

## 先说清楚什么叫"新架构"

新架构的标准是：**计算图的拓扑结构发生了根本性改变**，而不只是在现有图上加节点。

DELR的计算图是：
```
图像 → backbone → reference encoder → finetune encoder（M层并行self-attention）→ 19个坐标
```

真正的新架构要改变这个拓扑。

---

## 核心洞察：DuoAnno揭示了一个被忽视的结构

DuoAnno训练完之后，你得到了每个关键点的inter-observer disagreement。这不只是一个训练信号，它揭示了19个关键点之间的一种**天然的层级结构**：

```
确定层（低分歧）：Sella, Nasion, Gnathion...  → 医生高度一致，图像证据清晰
不确定层（高分歧）：Soft Pog, Labrale...       → 医生意见分散，图像证据模糊
```

**现有所有方法，包括DELR，完全无视这个结构。** 19个点平等地参与self-attention，平等地用local features精化，平等地被loss监督。

---

## 新架构：分层条件精化网络（HCRN）

**一句话：** 把19个关键点分成确定层和不确定层，先精化确定层，再以确定层的精化结果为条件精化不确定层。

这和DELR的本质区别是**信息流方向不同**：

```
DELR：
所有点同时精化 → self-attention（对称）→ 所有点同时更新

HCRN：
Stage 1：确定点独立精化（只用local features，不互相影响）
Stage 2：不确定点以精化后的确定点为条件（单向信息流）
```

---

## 为什么这个拓扑是合理的

有三个独立的支撑：

**临床支撑：** 医生标注头影测量的实际顺序就是先找骨性标志点（确定），再推断软组织点（不确定）。这是临床实践的标准流程，不是假设。

**数据支撑：** CeLR的per-landmark结果：No.1 Sella在Test2上MRE=0.41mm，No.16 Soft Pog MRE=3.73mm，相差9倍。不确定点的定位误差主要来自图像证据不足，而不是模型容量不足。给它更多的条件信息（确定点的精化坐标）是最直接的改进路径。

**消融支撑：** `no_local`比`no_finetune`更差，说明local sampling是核心。HCRN的Stage 2不只有local features，还有确定点的精化结果，信息更丰富，应该更好。

---

## 架构设计

### 关键点分组

分组不是固定的，而是由DuoAnno训练过程中统计的inter-observer disagreement决定：

```python
# 在训练集上统计每个关键点的平均observer disagreement
mean_disagreement = []
for i in range(19):
d = (y_junior[:, i] - y_senior[:, i]).norm(dim=-1).mean()
mean_disagreement.append(d.item())

# 按中位数分成两组
median_d = sorted(mean_disagreement)[9]
certain_idx   = [i for i,d in enumerate(mean_disagreement) if d <= median_d]
uncertain_idx = [i for i,d in enumerate(mean_disagreement) if d > median_d]
# 各约9-10个点
```

这个分组在训练前计算一次，训练中固定，不是动态的（简化实现，降低风险）。

### Stage 1：确定层独立精化

```python
class CertainStream(nn.Module):
"""
只处理确定点，用DELR的finetune encoder逻辑
关键：不做确定点之间的self-attention，只做local sampling
因为消融证明local sampling是主要贡献者，self-attention是次要的
"""
def __init__(self, dim, num_certain, num_layers=4):
super().__init__()
self.local_sampler = LocalSampler()  # 复用DELR的get_cls_embed
self.refine_layers = nn.ModuleList([
nn.Sequential(
nn.LayerNorm(dim),
nn.Linear(dim, dim),
nn.GELU(),
nn.Linear(dim, dim)
) for _ in range(num_layers)
])
self.coord_heads = nn.ModuleList([
CoordHead(dim) for _ in range(num_layers)
])
self.sigma_heads = nn.ModuleList([
SigmaHead(dim) for _ in range(num_layers)
])

def forward(self, feat_map, mu_R_certain, layer1, layer2, layer3,
output, sizes, wcl, inintv):
coords = mu_R_certain.detach()
token = self.local_sampler(feat_map, coords, ...)

outputs = []
for i in range(len(self.refine_layers)):
token = self.refine_layers[i](token)
delta = self.coord_heads[i](token)
coords = (coords + delta).clamp(1e-4, 1-1e-4)
sigma = self.sigma_heads[i](token)

# 更新local features
token = token + self.local_sampler(feat_map, coords, ...) * inintv
outputs.append((coords, sigma))

return outputs  # [(coords, sigma)] × num_layers
# 最终精化坐标和token供Stage 2使用
```

### Stage 2：不确定层条件精化

```python
class UncertainStream(nn.Module):
"""
处理不确定点，以确定点精化后的结果为条件
核心：cross-attention到确定点token，而不是self-attention
"""
def __init__(self, dim, num_uncertain, num_certain, num_layers=4):
super().__init__()
self.local_sampler = LocalSampler()

# 关键模块：cross-attention到确定点
self.certain_cross_attn = nn.MultiheadAttention(
embed_dim=dim, num_heads=8, batch_first=True
)
self.certain_cross_norm = nn.LayerNorm(dim)

self.refine_layers = nn.ModuleList([...])
self.coord_heads = nn.ModuleList([...])
self.sigma_heads = nn.ModuleList([...])

def forward(self, feat_map, mu_R_uncertain,
certain_final_coords, certain_final_token,
layer1, layer2, layer3, output, sizes, wcl, inintv):
"""
certain_final_coords: [B, N_certain, 2]  确定点的精化坐标
certain_final_token:  [B, N_certain, C]  确定点的精化token
"""
coords = mu_R_uncertain.detach()

# 初始token：local features + 从确定点获取的条件信息
local_feat = self.local_sampler(feat_map, coords, ...)

# ===== 核心：cross-attention到确定点 =====
# 问题：我现在的位置大概在哪，我周围的确定点精化后在哪里
# 这给了不确定点额外的空间约束信息
cond_feat = self.certain_cross_norm(local_feat)
cond_from_certain, _ = self.certain_cross_attn(
query=cond_feat,          # 不确定点问
key=certain_final_token,  # 确定点答（精化后的特征）
value=certain_final_token
)
token = local_feat + cond_from_certain
# ==========================================

outputs = []
for i in range(len(self.refine_layers)):
token = self.refine_layers[i](token)
delta = self.coord_heads[i](token)
coords = (coords + delta).clamp(1e-4, 1-1e-4)
sigma = self.sigma_heads[i](token)
token = token + self.local_sampler(feat_map, coords, ...) * inintv
outputs.append((coords, sigma))

return outputs
```

### 主网络整合

```python
def forward(self, x):
# Step1-3: backbone + feature processing + reference encoder（完全不动）
output1 = self.reference_encoder(...)  # [B, 19, 4]

# Step4: 按预计算的分组分离粗坐标
mu_R_certain   = output1[:, certain_idx, :2]
mu_R_uncertain = output1[:, uncertain_idx, :2]

# Step5: Stage 1 - 确定点独立精化
certain_outputs = self.certain_stream(
feat_map, mu_R_certain, ...
)
certain_final_coords, certain_final_sigma = certain_outputs[-1]
certain_final_token = self.certain_stream.last_token  # 保存中间token

# Step6: Stage 2 - 不确定点条件精化
uncertain_outputs = self.uncertain_stream(
feat_map, mu_R_uncertain,
certain_final_coords,    # 传入精化后的确定点坐标
certain_final_token,     # 传入精化后的确定点特征
...
)

# Step7: 合并所有层的输出
all_outputs = []
for lvl in range(num_layers):
full = torch.zeros(B, 19, 4)
full[:, certain_idx]   = cat_coord_sigma(certain_outputs[lvl])
full[:, uncertain_idx] = cat_coord_sigma(uncertain_outputs[lvl])
all_outputs.append(full)

return all_outputs, output1, hotmap
```

---

## 损失函数和DuoAnno/DisAug的结合

**损失函数：**

```python
# 确定点：标准DuoAnno（分歧小，两个标注接近）
L_certain = observer_nll(certain_pred,
y_junior[:, certain_idx],
y_senior[:, certain_idx],
alpha=0.3)  # 较小权重给双标注

# 不确定点：强化DuoAnno（分歧大，双标注更重要）
L_uncertain = observer_nll(uncertain_pred,
y_junior[:, uncertain_idx],
y_senior[:, uncertain_idx],
alpha=0.7)  # 更大权重给双标注

# Reference encoder
L_RE = standard_rle(output1, gt_mean)

L_total = L_RE + L_certain + L_uncertain
```

**DisAug的结合：**

DisAug对高分歧点做更激进的位置扰动——这些点恰好就是uncertain_idx里的点。DisAug在Stage 2的输入端引入更多的位置变化，让模型学会在更大的搜索空间里利用来自确定点的条件信息。两者的关系变成：**DisAug扩大了Stage 2需要处理的不确定性范围，cross-attention提供了处理这种不确定性所需的额外信息**。

---

## 论文贡献点

```
贡献1（问题发现）：
首次定量证明MRE和临床测量误差弱相关（散点图，r=0.31-0.55）

贡献2（数据分析）：
用inter-observer disagreement揭示了关键点之间天然的层级结构，
建立了"disagreement大的点应以disagreement小的点为条件"的理论依据

贡献3（新架构HCRN）：
提出分层条件精化网络，
将19个关键点分为确定层和不确定层，
用单向cross-attention代替对称self-attention，
这是第一个将observer disagreement结构显式编入架构拓扑的工作

贡献4（训练框架）：
DuoAnno定义分组依据，
DisAug增强不确定层的鲁棒性，
HCRN提供利用这两个信号的架构基础，
三者形成自洽的训练框架
```

---

## 和之前所有失败实验的本质区别

| 之前的尝试 | 失败原因 |
|-----------|---------|
| DuoDistRefine parallel head | 旁路，主路径不变，information flow没有改变 |
| DuoDistRefine 替换finetune | 丢失finetune的表示学习能力 |
| GALR | 在DELR外面加GNN，仍是对称结构 |
| UCSA | 在现有attention上加偏置，本质是修改而非新架构 |

**HCRN的本质不同：** 计算图拓扑改变了。Stage 1的确定点和Stage 2的不确定点之间有单向的、有语义含义的cross-attention连接。这个连接在DELR里根本不存在——DELR的self-attention是全对全的对称结构，HCRN是有向的层级结构。

---

先验证一件事：**DuoAnno训练完后，uncertain_idx里的点的observer disagreement是否显著高于certain_idx里的点。**

如果这个分组是有意义的（两组之间disagreement差异显著），整个架构的premise就成立了。你现在DuoAnno已经有结果，能不能直接用已有的σ值来验证这个分组？

1	# ------------------------------------------------------------------------------

8	from __future__ import absolute_import

19	import torch.nn as nn

21	import torch.utils.model_zoo as model_zoo
22	from functools import partial
23	from net.reg_loss import RLELoss

26	BN_MOMENTUM = 0.1
27	logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

30	class Block(nn.Module):
31	    def __init__(self, dim, num_heads, mlp_ratio=4.0, qkv_bias=True, norm_layer=nn.LayerNorm):
32	        super().__init__()
33	        self.norm1 = norm_layer(dim)
34	        self.attn = nn.MultiheadAttention(dim, num_heads, bias=qkv_bias, batch_first=True)
35	        self.norm2 = norm_layer(dim)
36	        hidden_dim = int(dim * mlp_ratio)
37	        self.mlp = nn.Sequential(
38	            nn.Linear(dim, hidden_dim),
39	            nn.GELU(),
40	            nn.Linear(hidden_dim, dim),
41	        )
42
43	    def forward(self, x):
44	        attn_input = self.norm1(x)
45	        attn_out, _ = self.attn(attn_input, attn_input, attn_input, need_weights=False)
46	        x = x + attn_out
47	        x = x + self.mlp(self.norm2(x))
48	        return x
49
50
51	def PositionalEncoding(max_len, d_model, device):
52	    encoding = torch.zeros(max_len, d_model, device=device)
53	    encoding.requires_grad = False
54	    pos = torch.arange(0, max_len, device=device).float().unsqueeze(dim=1)
55	    div_term = torch.arange(0, d_model, step=2, device=device).float()
56	    div_term = 10000 ** (div_term / d_model)
57	    encoding[:, 0::2] = torch.sin(pos / div_term)
58	    encoding[:, 1::2] = torch.cos(pos / div_term)
59	    return encoding
60
61
62	def get_1d_sincos_pos_embed_from_grid(embed_dim, pos):
63	    assert embed_dim % 2 == 0
64	    omega = np.arange(embed_dim // 2, dtype=np.float32)
65	    omega /= embed_dim / 2.
66	    omega = 1. / 10000**omega
67	    pos = pos.reshape(-1)
68	    out = np.einsum('m,d->md', pos, omega)
69	    emb_sin = np.sin(out)
70	    emb_cos = np.cos(out)
71	    return np.concatenate([emb_sin, emb_cos], axis=1)
72
73
74	def get_2d_sincos_pos_embed_from_grid(embed_dim, grid):
75	    assert embed_dim % 2 == 0
76	    emb_h = get_1d_sincos_pos_embed_from_grid(embed_dim // 2, grid[0])
77	    emb_w = get_1d_sincos_pos_embed_from_grid(embed_dim // 2, grid[1])
78	    return np.concatenate([emb_h, emb_w], axis=1)
79
80
81	def get_2d_sincos_pos_embed(embed_dim, grid_size, cls_token=False):
82	    grid_h = np.arange(grid_size[1], dtype=np.float32)
83	    grid_w = np.arange(grid_size[0], dtype=np.float32)
84	    grid = np.meshgrid(grid_w, grid_h)
85	    grid = np.stack(grid, axis=0).reshape([2, 1, grid_size[1], grid_size[0]])
86	    pos_embed = get_2d_sincos_pos_embed_from_grid(embed_dim, grid)
87	    if cls_token:
88	        pos_embed = np.concatenate([np.zeros([1, embed_dim]), pos_embed], axis=0)
89	    return pos_embed
90
91	model_urls = {
92	    'resnet18': 'https://download.pytorch.org/models/resnet18-5c106cde.pth',
93	    'resnet34': 'https://download.pytorch.org/models/resnet34-333f7ec4.pth',
94	    'resnet50': 'https://download.pytorch.org/models/resnet50-19c8e357.pth',
95	    'resnet101': 'https://download.pytorch.org/models/resnet101-5d3b4d8f.pth',
96	    'resnet152': 'https://download.pytorch.org/models/resnet152-b121ed2d.pth',
97	}
98	def inverse_sigmoid(x, eps=1e-5):
99	    """Inverse function of sigmoid.
100	    Args:
101	        x (Tensor): The tensor to do the
102	            inverse.
103	        eps (float): EPS avoid numerical
104	            overflow. Defaults 1e-5.
105	    Returns:
106	        Tensor: The x has passed the inverse
107	            function of sigmoid, has same
108	            shape with input.
109	    """
110	    x = x.clamp(min=0, max=1)
111	    x1 = x.clamp(min=eps)
112	    x2 = (1 - x).clamp(min=eps)
113	    return torch.log(x1 / x2)
114	def get_proposal_pos_embed(proposals,
115	                           num_pos_feats=128,
116	                           temperature=10000):
117	    """Get the position embedding of proposal."""
118	    num_pos_feats = num_pos_feats // 2
119	    scale = 2 * math.pi
120	    dim_t = torch.arange(
121	        num_pos_feats, dtype=torch.float32, device=proposals.device)
122	    dim_t = temperature ** (2 * (dim_t // 2) / num_pos_feats)
123	    # N, L, 2
124	    proposals = proposals * scale
125
126	    # N, L, 2, 128
127	    pos = proposals[:, :, :, None] / dim_t
128	    # N, L, 2, 64, 2
129	    pos = torch.stack((pos[:, :, :, 0::2].sin(), pos[:, :, :, 1::2].cos()), dim=4).flatten(2)
130	    return pos
131
132	def get_cls_embed(layer1, layer2, layer3, output, coords, sizes, wcl, n_landmarks=19):
133	    layer1 = layer1.view(-1, sizes[2], sizes[3], sizes[1]).permute(0, 3, 1, 2)
134	    layer2 = layer2.view(-1, sizes[2], sizes[3], sizes[1]).permute(0, 3, 1, 2)
135	    layer3 = layer3.view(-1, sizes[2], sizes[3], sizes[1]).permute(0, 3, 1, 2)
136	    output = output.view(-1, sizes[2], sizes[3], sizes[1]).permute(0, 3, 1, 2)
137
138
139	    coords = coords.view(-1, 1, n_landmarks, 2) *2 -1
140	    coords = coords.clip(-1, 1)
141	    cls1 = F.grid_sample(layer1, coords)
142	    cls2 = F.grid_sample(layer2, coords)
143	    cls3 = F.grid_sample(layer3, coords)
144	    cls4 = F.grid_sample(output, coords)
145
146	    cls1 = cls1.squeeze(dim=2).permute(0, 2, 1)
147	    cls2 = cls2.squeeze(dim=2).permute(0, 2, 1)
148	    cls3 = cls3.squeeze(dim=2).permute(0, 2, 1)
149	    cls4 = cls4.squeeze(dim=2).permute(0, 2, 1)
150
151	    cls = cls1*wcl[1] + cls2*wcl[2] + cls3*wcl[3] + cls4*wcl[0]
152
153	    return cls
154
155	def conv3x3(in_planes, out_planes, stride=1):
156	    """3x3 convolution with padding"""
157	    return nn.Conv2d(in_planes, out_planes, kernel_size=3, stride=stride,
158	                     padding=1, bias=False)
159
160
161	class BasicBlock(nn.Module):
162	    expansion = 1
163
164	    def __init__(self, inplanes, planes, stride=1, downsample=None):
165	        super(BasicBlock, self).__init__()
166	        self.conv1 = conv3x3(inplanes, planes, stride)
167	        self.bn1 = nn.BatchNorm2d(planes, momentum=BN_MOMENTUM)
168	        self.relu = nn.ReLU(inplace=True)
169	        self.conv2 = conv3x3(planes, planes)
170	        self.bn2 = nn.BatchNorm2d(planes, momentum=BN_MOMENTUM)
171	        self.downsample = downsample
172	        self.stride = stride
173
174	    def forward(self, x):
175	        residual = x
176
177	        out = self.conv1(x)
178	        out = self.bn1(out)
179	        out = self.relu(out)
180
181	        out = self.conv2(out)
182	        out = self.bn2(out)
183
184	        if self.downsample is not None:
185	            residual = self.downsample(x)
186
187	        out += residual
188	        out = self.relu(out)
189
190	        return out
191
192
193	class Bottleneck(nn.Module):
194	    expansion = 4
195
196	    def __init__(self, inplanes, planes, stride=1, downsample=None):
197	        super(Bottleneck, self).__init__()
198	        self.conv1 = nn.Conv2d(inplanes, planes, kernel_size=1, bias=False)
199	        self.bn1 = nn.BatchNorm2d(planes, momentum=BN_MOMENTUM)
200	        self.conv2 = nn.Conv2d(planes, planes, kernel_size=3, stride=stride,
201	                               padding=1, bias=False)
202	        self.bn2 = nn.BatchNorm2d(planes, momentum=BN_MOMENTUM)
203	        self.conv3 = nn.Conv2d(planes, planes * self.expansion, kernel_size=1,
204	                               bias=False)
205	        self.bn3 = nn.BatchNorm2d(planes * self.expansion,
206	                                  momentum=BN_MOMENTUM)
207	        self.relu = nn.ReLU(inplace=True)
208	        self.downsample = downsample
209	        self.stride = stride
210
211	    def forward(self, x):
212	        residual = x
213
214	        out = self.conv1(x)
215	        out = self.bn1(out)
216	        out = self.relu(out)
217
218	        out = self.conv2(out)
219	        out = self.bn2(out)
220	        out = self.relu(out)
221
222	        out = self.conv3(out)
223	        out = self.bn3(out)
224
225	        if self.downsample is not None:
226	            residual = self.downsample(x)
227
228	        out += residual
229	        out = self.relu(out)
230
231	        return out
232
233

239
240	def fill_up_weights(up):
241	    w = up.weight.data
242	    f = math.ceil(w.size(2) / 2)
243	    c = (2 * f - 1 - f % 2) / (2. * f)
244	    for i in range(w.size(2)):
245	        for j in range(w.size(3)):
246	            w[0, 0, i, j] = \
247	                (1 - math.fabs(i / f - c)) * (1 - math.fabs(j / f - c))
248	    for c in range(1, w.size(0)):
249	        w[c, 0, :, :] = w[0, 0, :, :]
250
251	def fill_fc_weights(layers):
252	    for m in layers.modules():
253	        if isinstance(m, nn.Conv2d):
254	            nn.init.normal_(m.weight, std=0.001)
255	            # torch.nn.init.kaiming_normal_(m.weight.data, nonlinearity='relu')
256	            # torch.nn.init.xavier_normal_(m.weight.data)
257	            if m.bias is not None:
258	                nn.init.constant_(m.bias, 0)

260
261	BN_MOMENTUM = 0.1
262	resnet_spec = {18: (BasicBlock, [2, 2, 2, 2]),
263	               34: (BasicBlock, [3, 4, 6, 3]),
264	               50: (Bottleneck, [3, 4, 6, 3]),
265	               101: (Bottleneck, [3, 4, 16, 3]),
266	               152: (Bottleneck, [3, 8, 36, 3])}
267	class PoseResNet(nn.Module):
268
269	    def __init__(self, num_layers, heads, head_conv):
270	        super(PoseResNet, self).__init__()
271	        block, layers = resnet_spec[num_layers]
272	        self.inplanes = 64
273	        self.heads = heads
274	        self.deconv_with_bias = False
275
276	        super(PoseResNet, self).__init__()
277	        self.conv1 = nn.Conv2d(3, 64, kernel_size=7, stride=2, padding=3,
278	                               bias=False)
279	        self.bn1 = nn.BatchNorm2d(64, momentum=BN_MOMENTUM)
280	        self.relu = nn.ReLU(inplace=True)
281
282
283	        self.maxpool = nn.MaxPool2d(kernel_size=3, stride=2, padding=1)
284	        self.layer1 = self._make_layer(block, 64, layers[0])
285	        self.layer2 = self._make_layer(block, 128, layers[1], stride=2)
286	        self.layer3 = self._make_layer(block, 256, layers[2], stride=2)
287	        self.layer4 = self._make_layer(block, 512, layers[3], stride=2)
288	        print("")
289
290	        # used for deconv layers
291
292	    def _make_layer(self, block, planes, blocks, stride=1):
293	        downsample = None
294	        if stride != 1 or self.inplanes != planes * block.expansion:
295	            downsample = nn.Sequential(
296	                nn.Conv2d(self.inplanes, planes * block.expansion,
297	                          kernel_size=1, stride=stride, bias=False),
298	                nn.BatchNorm2d(planes * block.expansion, momentum=BN_MOMENTUM),
299	            )
300
301	        layers = []
302	        layers.append(block(self.inplanes, planes, stride, downsample))
303	        self.inplanes = planes * block.expansion
304	        for i in range(1, blocks):
305	            layers.append(block(self.inplanes, planes))
306
307	        return nn.Sequential(*layers)
308
309
310
311	    def forward(self, x):
312	        conv1 = self.conv1(x)
313	        conv1 = self.bn1(conv1)
314	        conv1 = self.relu(conv1)
315
316	        x = self.maxpool(conv1)
317
318	        layer1 = self.layer1(x)
319	        layer2 = self.layer2(layer1)
320	        layer3 = self.layer3(layer2)
321	        layer4 = self.layer4(layer3)
322
323
324
325	        return layer1, layer2, layer3, layer4
326
327	    def init_weights(self, num_layers):
328	        if 1:
329	            url = model_urls['resnet{}'.format(num_layers)]
330	            pretrained_state_dict = model_zoo.load_url(url)
331	            print('=> loading pretrained model {}'.format(url))
332	            self.load_state_dict(pretrained_state_dict, strict=False)
333	            print('=> init deconv weights from normal distribution')

335
336	class Linear_with_norm(nn.Module):
337	    def __init__(self, in_channel, out_channel, bias=True, norm=True):
338	        super(Linear_with_norm, self).__init__()
339	        self.bias = bias
340	        self.norm = norm
341	        self.linear = nn.Linear(in_channel, out_channel, bias)
342	        nn.init.xavier_uniform_(self.linear.weight, gain=0.01)
343
344	    def forward(self, x):
345	        y = x.matmul(self.linear.weight.t())
346
347	        if self.norm:
348	            x_norm = torch.norm(x, dim=-1, keepdim=True)
349	            y = y / x_norm
350
351	        if self.bias:
352	            y = y + self.linear.bias
353	        return y
354
355
356	def _load_hcrn_v1_groups(num_landmarks=19):
357	    """Load train-only hierarchy groups, with the current canonical fallback."""
358	    default_certain = [11, 10, 8, 0, 6, 7, 1, 16, 13, 14]
359	    default_uncertain = [17, 18, 12, 5, 2, 4, 3, 9, 15]
360	    group_path = os.environ.get("DELR_HCRN_GROUP_PATH", "")
361	    if group_path and os.path.exists(group_path):
362	        with open(group_path, "r") as f:
363	            obj = json.load(f)
364	        certain = obj.get("certain_idx", obj.get("certain", default_certain))
365	        uncertain = obj.get("uncertain_idx", obj.get("uncertain", default_uncertain))
366	    else:
367	        certain = default_certain
368	        uncertain = default_uncertain
369
370	    all_idx = sorted(list(certain) + list(uncertain))
371	    if all_idx != list(range(num_landmarks)):
372	        raise ValueError(f"Invalid HCRN-v1 groups: certain={certain}, uncertain={uncertain}")
373	    return certain, uncertain
374
375
376	def _make_coord_branch(dim):
377	    layers = []
378	    for _ in range(2):
379	        layers.append(nn.Linear(dim, dim))
380	        layers.append(nn.ReLU())
381	    layers.append(nn.Linear(dim, 2))
382	    return nn.Sequential(*layers)
383
384
385	def _make_sigma_branch(dim):
386	    return nn.Sequential(
387	        nn.Linear(dim, dim),
388	        nn.Linear(dim, dim),
389	        Linear_with_norm(dim, 2, norm=False),
390	    )
391
392
393	def _make_refine_mlp(dim):
394	    return nn.Sequential(
395	        nn.LayerNorm(dim),
396	        nn.Linear(dim, dim),
397	        nn.GELU(),
398	        nn.Linear(dim, dim),
399	    )
400
401
402	def _make_fuse_mlp(dim):
403	    return nn.Sequential(
404	        nn.LayerNorm(dim * 2),
405	        nn.Linear(dim * 2, dim),
406	        nn.GELU(),
407	        nn.Linear(dim, dim),
408	    )

411	class get_model(nn.Module):
412
413	    def __init__(self, num_layers, heads=None, head_conv=256, NLayer1=4, NLayer2=4, numchannel=512, n_landmarks=None):
414	        super(get_model, self).__init__()
415	        self.n_landmarks = n_landmarks if n_landmarks is not None else cfg.PointNms
416	        self.NLayer1 = NLayer1
417	        self.NLayer = NLayer2
418
419
420	        model = PoseResNet(num_layers, heads, head_conv=head_conv)
421	        model.init_weights(num_layers)
422	        self.backone = model
423
424
425	        self.out1 = nn.Conv2d(in_channels=numchannel, out_channels=1, kernel_size=1, stride=1)
426
427	        self.sizem = torch.tensor([cfg.IMG_Height // 32, cfg.IMG_Width // 32]).int()
428	        self.grid_vx = torch.zeros((1, 2, self.sizem[0], self.sizem[1])).float()
429	        self.grid_vy = torch.zeros((1, 2, self.sizem[0], self.sizem[1])).float()
430	        self.encoder_embed = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(1, self.n_landmarks, numchannel), requires_grad=False)
431
432	        self.conv1 = nn.Conv2d(in_channels=64, out_channels=numchannel, kernel_size=1, stride=1, bias=False)
433	        self.conv2 = nn.Conv2d(in_channels=128, out_channels=numchannel, kernel_size=1, stride=1, bias=False)
434	        self.conv3 = nn.Conv2d(in_channels=256, out_channels=numchannel, kernel_size=1, stride=1, bias=False)
435	        self.bn1 = nn.BatchNorm2d(numchannel, momentum=BN_MOMENTUM)
436	        self.bn2 = nn.BatchNorm2d(numchannel, momentum=BN_MOMENTUM)
437	        self.bn3 = nn.BatchNorm2d(numchannel, momentum=BN_MOMENTUM)
438	        self.conv4 = nn.Conv2d(in_channels=64, out_channels=numchannel, kernel_size=1, stride=1, bias=False)
439	        self.conv5 = nn.Conv2d(in_channels=128, out_channels=numchannel, kernel_size=1, stride=1, bias=False)
440	        self.conv6 = nn.Conv2d(in_channels=256, out_channels=numchannel, kernel_size=1, stride=1, bias=False)
441
442
443	        self.inintv = nn.Parameter(torch.tensor([1.0]), requires_grad=True)
444	        self.pg = nn.Parameter(torch.tensor([1, 0.8, 0.6, 0.4]), requires_grad=True)
445	        self.wg = nn.Parameter(torch.tensor([1, 0.8, 0.6, 0.4]), requires_grad=True)
446	        self.wcl = nn.Parameter(torch.tensor([1, 0.8, 0.6, 0.4]), requires_grad=True)
447	        self.pos_embedly1 = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(1, self.sizem[0] * 8,self.sizem[1]*8, numchannel//8), requires_grad=False)
448	        self.pos_embedly2 = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(1, self.sizem[0] * 4,self.sizem[1]*4, numchannel//4), requires_grad=False)
449	        self.pos_embedly3 = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(1, self.sizem[0] * 2,self.sizem[1]*2, numchannel//2), requires_grad=False)
450	        self.pos_embed = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(1, self.sizem[0] *self.sizem[1], numchannel), requires_grad=False)  # fixed sin-cos embedding
451	        norm_layer = partial(nn.LayerNorm, eps=1e-6)
452
453
454	        self.InitBlock = nn.ModuleList([
455	            Block(dim=numchannel, num_heads=numchannel//64, mlp_ratio=2, qkv_bias=True, norm_layer=norm_layer)
456	            for i in range(self.NLayer1)])
457	        self.linear11 = nn.Linear(numchannel, 256)
458	        self.linear12 = nn.Linear(256, 4)
459
460	        self.transblock = nn.ModuleList([
461	            Block(dim=numchannel, num_heads=numchannel//64, mlp_ratio=2, qkv_bias=True, norm_layer=norm_layer)
462	            for i in range(self.NLayer)])
463	        # self.linear21 = nn.Linear(numchannel, 256)
464	        # self.linear22 = nn.Linear(256, 4)
465
466	        fc_coord_branch = []
467	        for _ in range(2):
468	            fc_coord_branch.append(nn.Linear(numchannel, numchannel))
469	            fc_coord_branch.append(nn.ReLU())
470	        fc_coord_branch.append(nn.Linear(numchannel, 2))
471	        fc_coord_branch = nn.Sequential(*fc_coord_branch)
472	        self.fc_coord_branches = self._get_clones(fc_coord_branch, self.NLayer)
473	        self.fc_coord_output_branches = self._get_clones(fc_coord_branch, self.NLayer)
474
475	        fc_sigma_branch = []
476	        for _ in range(2):
477	            fc_sigma_branch.append(nn.Linear(numchannel, numchannel))
478	        fc_sigma_branch.append(Linear_with_norm(numchannel, 2, norm=False))
479	        fc_sigma_branch = nn.Sequential(*fc_sigma_branch)
480	        self.fc_sigma_branches = self._get_clones(fc_sigma_branch, self.NLayer)
481
482	        # HCRN-v1 true two-stage hierarchy. When enabled, this replaces
483	        # the original finetune encoder instead of acting as a post-hoc adapter.
484	        self.hcrn_v1 = os.environ.get("DELR_HCRN_V1", "0") == "1"
485	        certain_idx, uncertain_idx = _load_hcrn_v1_groups(self.n_landmarks)
486	        self.register_buffer("hcrn_v1_certain_idx", torch.tensor(certain_idx, dtype=torch.long))
487	        self.register_buffer("hcrn_v1_uncertain_idx", torch.tensor(uncertain_idx, dtype=torch.long))
488	        self.hcrn_v1_group_path = os.environ.get("DELR_HCRN_GROUP_PATH", "")
489
490	        self.hcrn_certain_refine = nn.ModuleList([
491	            _make_refine_mlp(numchannel) for _ in range(self.NLayer)
492	        ])
493	        self.hcrn_certain_coord_branches = nn.ModuleList([
494	            _make_coord_branch(numchannel) for _ in range(self.NLayer)
495	        ])
496	        self.hcrn_certain_coord_output_branches = nn.ModuleList([
497	            _make_coord_branch(numchannel) for _ in range(self.NLayer)
498	        ])
499	        self.hcrn_certain_sigma_branches = nn.ModuleList([
500	            _make_sigma_branch(numchannel) for _ in range(self.NLayer)
501	        ])
502
503	        self.hcrn_uncertain_q_norm = nn.ModuleList([
504	            nn.LayerNorm(numchannel) for _ in range(self.NLayer)
505	        ])
506	        self.hcrn_uncertain_kv_norm = nn.ModuleList([
507	            nn.LayerNorm(numchannel) for _ in range(self.NLayer)
508	        ])
509	        self.hcrn_uncertain_cross_attn = nn.ModuleList([
510	            nn.MultiheadAttention(numchannel, numchannel // 64, batch_first=True)
511	            for _ in range(self.NLayer)
512	        ])
513	        self.hcrn_uncertain_fuse = nn.ModuleList([
514	            _make_fuse_mlp(numchannel) for _ in range(self.NLayer)
515	        ])
516	        self.hcrn_uncertain_coord_branches = nn.ModuleList([
517	            _make_coord_branch(numchannel) for _ in range(self.NLayer)
518	        ])
519	        self.hcrn_uncertain_coord_output_branches = nn.ModuleList([
520	            _make_coord_branch(numchannel) for _ in range(self.NLayer)
521	        ])
522	        self.hcrn_uncertain_sigma_branches = nn.ModuleList([
523	            _make_sigma_branch(numchannel) for _ in range(self.NLayer)
524	        ])
525

530	                 size_average=True,
531	                 residual=True,

534	                 size_average=True,
535	                 residual=True,
536	                 q_dis='laplace')

541	    def initialize_weights(self):
542	        # initialization
543	        # initialize (and freeze) pos_embed by sin-cos embedding
544	        pos_embed = get_2d_sincos_pos_embed(self.pos_embed.shape[-1], self.sizem, cls_token=False)
545	        self.pos_embed.data.copy_(torch.from_numpy(pos_embed).float().unsqueeze(0))
546
547	        pos_embedly1 = get_2d_sincos_pos_embed(self.pos_embedly1.shape[-1], self.sizem*8, cls_token=False)
548	        pos_embedly1 = pos_embedly1.reshape(self.sizem[0]*8, self.sizem[1]*8, 64)
549	        self.pos_embedly1.data.copy_(torch.from_numpy(pos_embedly1).float().unsqueeze(0))
550
551
552	        pos_embedly2 = get_2d_sincos_pos_embed(self.pos_embedly2.shape[-1], self.sizem*4, cls_token=False)
553	        pos_embedly2 = pos_embedly2.reshape(self.sizem[0] * 4, self.sizem[1] * 4, 128)
554	        self.pos_embedly2.data.copy_(torch.from_numpy(pos_embedly2).float().unsqueeze(0))
555
556	        pos_embedly3 = get_2d_sincos_pos_embed(self.pos_embedly3.shape[-1], self.sizem*2, cls_token=False)
557	        pos_embedly3 = pos_embedly3.reshape(self.sizem[0] * 2, self.sizem[1] * 2, 256)
558	        self.pos_embedly3.data.copy_(torch.from_numpy(pos_embedly3).float().unsqueeze(0))
559
560
561	        device = torch.device("cuda")
562	        pos_embed1 = PositionalEncoding(self.encoder_embed.shape[1], self.encoder_embed.shape[2], device)
563	        self.encoder_embed.data.copy_(pos_embed1.float().unsqueeze(0))
564
565	    def _get_clones(self, module, N):
566	        return nn.ModuleList([copy.deepcopy(module) for i in range(N)])
567
568
569	    def _init_weights(self, m):
570	        if isinstance(m, nn.Linear):
571	            # we use xavier_uniform following official JAX ViT:
572	            torch.nn.init.xavier_uniform_(m.weight)
573	            if isinstance(m, nn.Linear) and m.bias is not None:
574	                nn.init.constant_(m.bias, 0)
575	        elif isinstance(m, nn.LayerNorm):
576	            nn.init.constant_(m.bias, 0)
577	            nn.init.constant_(m.weight, 1.0)
578
579	    def forward_hcrn_v1(self, output1, hotmap, layer1, layer2, layer3, output, sizes, batch_size):
580	        """True two-stage HCRN: certain stream first, uncertain stream second."""
581	        b = batch_size
582	        certain_idx = self.hcrn_v1_certain_idx
583	        uncertain_idx = self.hcrn_v1_uncertain_idx
584	        n_certain = int(certain_idx.numel())
585	        n_uncertain = int(uncertain_idx.numel())
586
587	        def sample_local(coords, n_points):
588	            return get_cls_embed(
589	                layer1, layer2, layer3, output,
590	                coords.detach(), sizes, self.wcl, n_points,
591	            )
592
593	        # Stage 1: certain landmarks refine first, with no access to uncertain tokens.
594	        coords_c = output1[:, certain_idx, :2].detach().clip(0, 1)
595	        embed_c = self.encoder_embed[:, certain_idx, :].expand(b, -1, -1)
596	        token_c = embed_c + sample_local(coords_c, n_certain) * self.inintv
597	        certain_outputs = []
598
599	        for i in range(self.NLayer):
600	            token_c = token_c + self.hcrn_certain_refine[i](token_c)
601	            coord_logits = self.hcrn_certain_coord_branches[i](token_c) + inverse_sigmoid(coords_c)
602	            coords_c_next = coord_logits.sigmoid()
603	            sigma_c = self.hcrn_certain_sigma_branches[i](token_c)
604	            coord_out_c = coords_c_next + self.hcrn_certain_coord_output_branches[i](token_c)
605	            certain_outputs.append(torch.cat([coord_out_c, sigma_c], dim=-1))
606
607	            coords_c = coords_c_next
608	            token_c = token_c + embed_c + sample_local(coords_c, n_certain) * self.inintv
609
610	        certain_final_token = token_c.detach()
611
612	        # Stage 2: uncertain landmarks condition on refined certain tokens.
613	        coords_u = output1[:, uncertain_idx, :2].detach().clip(0, 1)
614	        embed_u = self.encoder_embed[:, uncertain_idx, :].expand(b, -1, -1)
615	        token_u = embed_u + sample_local(coords_u, n_uncertain) * self.inintv
616	        uncertain_outputs = []
617	        attn_records = []
618
619	        for i in range(self.NLayer):
620	            q = self.hcrn_uncertain_q_norm[i](token_u)

bash -lc cd /mnt/data/hcrn_audit/hcrn_v1_key_package/code
nl -ba ceph_reg_refine_net.py | sed -n '620,820p'

**tool：**

620	            q = self.hcrn_uncertain_q_norm[i](token_u)
621	            kv = self.hcrn_uncertain_kv_norm[i](certain_final_token)
622	            cond, attn = self.hcrn_uncertain_cross_attn[i](
623	                query=q,
624	                key=kv,
625	                value=kv,
626	                need_weights=True,
627	                average_attn_weights=True,
628	            )
629	            token_u = self.hcrn_uncertain_fuse[i](torch.cat([token_u, cond], dim=-1))
630	            coord_logits = self.hcrn_uncertain_coord_branches[i](token_u) + inverse_sigmoid(coords_u)
631	            coords_u_next = coord_logits.sigmoid()
632	            sigma_u = self.hcrn_uncertain_sigma_branches[i](token_u)
633	            coord_out_u = coords_u_next + self.hcrn_uncertain_coord_output_branches[i](token_u)
634	            uncertain_outputs.append(torch.cat([coord_out_u, sigma_u], dim=-1))
635	            attn_records.append(attn.detach())
636
637	            coords_u = coords_u_next
638	            token_u = token_u + embed_u + sample_local(coords_u, n_uncertain) * self.inintv
639
640	        outputs = []
641	        for i in range(self.NLayer):
642	            full = torch.zeros(
643	                b, self.n_landmarks, 4,
644	                device=output1.device,
645	                dtype=certain_outputs[i].dtype,
646	            )
647	            full = full.index_copy(1, certain_idx, certain_outputs[i])
648	            full = full.index_copy(1, uncertain_idx, uncertain_outputs[i])
649	            outputs.append(full)
650
651	        self.last_hcrn_v1_attn = attn_records
652	        return outputs, output1, hotmap
653
654	    def forward(self, x):
655	        layer1, layer2, layer3, output = self.backone(x)
656	        hotmap = self.out1(output)
657
658	        b, c, h, w = output.shape
659	        pos1 = self.pos_embedly1.expand(b, -1, -1, -1).permute(0, 3, 1, 2)
660	        pos2 = self.pos_embedly2.expand(b, -1, -1, -1).permute(0, 3, 1, 2)
661	        pos3 = self.pos_embedly3.expand(b, -1, -1, -1).permute(0, 3, 1, 2)
662
663	        layer1 = self.bn1(self.conv1(F.interpolate(layer1, (self.sizem[0], self.sizem[1])))).view(b, c, h* w).permute(0, 2, 1)
664	        layer2 = self.bn2(self.conv2(F.interpolate(layer2, (self.sizem[0], self.sizem[1])))).view(b, c, h* w).permute(0, 2, 1)
665	        layer3 = self.bn3(self.conv3(F.interpolate(layer3, (self.sizem[0], self.sizem[1])))).view(b, c, h* w).permute(0, 2, 1)
666
667
668	        pos1 = self.conv4(F.interpolate(pos1, (self.sizem[0], self.sizem[1]))).view(b, c, h* w).permute(0, 2, 1)
669	        pos2 = self.conv5(F.interpolate(pos2, (self.sizem[0], self.sizem[1]))).view(b, c, h* w).permute(0, 2, 1)
670	        pos3 = self.conv6(F.interpolate(pos3, (self.sizem[0], self.sizem[1]))).view(b, c, h* w).permute(0, 2, 1)
671
672	        layer1 = layer1 + pos1
673	        layer2 = layer2 + pos2
674	        layer3 = layer3 + pos3
675
676	        x4 = output.view(b, c, h* w).permute(0, 2, 1)
677	        sizes = [b, c, h, w]
678	        #################################################################
679	        inc = x4 + self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1)
680	        inc = torch.cat([inc,  self.encoder_embed.expand(b, -1, -1)], dim=1)
681	        pos = torch.cat([self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1), self.encoder_embed.expand(b, -1, -1)], dim=1)
682
683	        xcs = []
684	        for cpb in self.InitBlock:
685	            inc = cpb(inc)
686	            xcs.append(inc)
687	            inc = inc+pos
688	        output1 = self.linear12(F.relu(self.linear11(xcs[-1][:, -self.n_landmarks:, :])))
689	        #################################################################
690
691	        # xc = (x4 + self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1))
692	        xc = (x4 + self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1))*self.wg[0] + layer1*self.wg[1] + layer2*self.wg[2] + layer3*self.wg[3]
693	        # inint_coords = get_proposal_pos_embed(output1[:, :, :2].detach(), num_pos_feats=512, temperature=10000)
694	        output = x4 + self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1)
695	        if self.hcrn_v1:
696	            return self.forward_hcrn_v1(output1, hotmap, layer1, layer2, layer3, output, sizes, b)
697	        inint_coords = get_cls_embed(layer1, layer2, layer3, output, output1[:, :, :2].detach(), sizes, self.wcl, self.n_landmarks)
698
699	        encoder_embed = self.encoder_embed.expand(b, -1, -1)  + inint_coords * self.inintv
700	        # pos = torch.cat([self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1),encoder_embed], dim=1)
701	        # pos = torch.cat([self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1) * self.pg[0] + pos1 * self.pg[1] + pos2 * self.pg[2] + pos3 * self.pg[3], encoder_embed], dim=1)
702
703	        hs = []
704	        inter_references = []
705	        xc_ = torch.cat([xc, encoder_embed], dim=1)
706	        reference_points = output1[:, :, :2].detach().clip(0, 1)
707	        init_reference = reference_points
708	        for i, cpb in enumerate(self.transblock):
709	            xc_ = cpb(xc_)
710	            tmp = self.fc_coord_branches[i](xc_[:, -self.n_landmarks:, :])
711
712	            new_reference_points = tmp + inverse_sigmoid(reference_points)
713	            new_reference_points = new_reference_points.sigmoid()
714
715	            reference_points = new_reference_points
716
717	            inint_coords = get_cls_embed(layer1, layer2, layer3, output, new_reference_points.detach(), sizes, self.wcl, self.n_landmarks)
718	            # inint_coords = get_proposal_pos_embed(new_reference_points.detach(), num_pos_feats=512, temperature=10000)
719	            encoder_embed = self.encoder_embed.expand(b, -1, -1) + inint_coords * self.inintv
720	            pos = torch.cat([self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1) * self.pg[0] + pos1 * self.pg[1] + pos2 * self.pg[2] + pos3 * self.pg[3], encoder_embed], dim=1)
721	            xc_ = xc_ + pos
722
723	            inter_references.append(reference_points)
724	            hs.append(xc_[:, -self.n_landmarks:, :])
725	        outputs = []
726	        for lvl in range(len(inter_references)):
727	            if lvl == 0:
728	                reference = init_reference
729	            else:
730	                reference = inter_references[lvl - 1]
731	            reference = inverse_sigmoid(reference)
732
733	            tmp = self.fc_coord_branches[lvl](hs[lvl])
734	            tmp = tmp + reference
735
736
737	            outputs_sigma = self.fc_sigma_branches[lvl](hs[lvl])
738
739
740	            outputs_coord = tmp.sigmoid()
741	            delta_coord_output = self.fc_coord_output_branches[lvl](hs[lvl])
742	            outputs_coord = (outputs_coord + delta_coord_output)
743
744	            outputs_coord = torch.cat([outputs_coord, outputs_sigma], dim=-1)
745	            outputs.append(outputs_coord)
746
747	        # output = F.relu(self.linear21(xcs[-1][:, -encoder_embed.shape[1]:, :]))
748	        # output = self.linear22(output)
749
750
751	        return outputs, output1, hotmap
752
753
754	if __name__ == "__main__":
755
756	    num_layers =34
757	    head_conv = 256
758	    heads = {'hm': 1, 'class': cfg.PointNms}
759	    model = PoseResNet(num_layers, heads, head_conv=head_conv)

38	class IOStream():
39	    def __init__(self, path):
40	        self.f = open(path, 'a')
41
42	    def cprint(self, text):
43	        print(text)
44	        self.f.write(text+'\n')
45	        self.f.flush()
46
47	    def close(self):
48	        self.f.close()

51	def observer_aware_rle(loss_fn, output, mean_target, observer_target, target_mode, alpha):
52	    """Mean-anchored dual-annotation RLE for DuoAnno second-model control."""
53	    mean_loss = loss_fn(output, mean_target)
54	    if target_mode == "mean":
55	        return mean_loss
56	    if observer_target is None:
57	        raise ValueError("observer_target is required for observer-aware target modes")
58
59	    observer_loss = 0.5 * (
60	        loss_fn(output, observer_target[:, 0]) +
61	        loss_fn(output, observer_target[:, 1])
62	    )
63	    if target_mode == "observer_avg_nll":
64	        return observer_loss
65	    if target_mode == "observer_mixed_nll":
66	        return (1.0 - alpha) * mean_loss + alpha * observer_loss
67	    raise ValueError(f"Unsupported target_mode: {target_mode}")
68
69
70	def train(args, io):
71
72
73	    file_path = TRAIN_IMG_DIR
74	    label_path = ANNOTATION_DIR
75
76	    train_dataset = TrainData(file_path, label_path, target_mode=args.target_mode)
77	    if args.limit_train_samples > 0:
78	        train_dataset = Subset(train_dataset, range(args.limit_train_samples))
79	    train_loader = DataLoader(train_dataset,
80	                              num_workers=args.num_workers,
81	                              batch_size=args.batch_size, shuffle=True, drop_last=True)
82	    file_path = TEST1_IMG_DIR
83	    label_path = ANNOTATION_DIR
84	    test_loader = DataLoader(TestData(file_path, label_path), num_workers=0,
85	                             batch_size=1, shuffle=False, drop_last=False)
86
87	    # Try to load models
88	    num_layers =34
89	    head_conv = 256
90	    heads = {'hm': 1, 'class': cfg.PointNms}
91	    model = get_model(num_layers=num_layers, heads=heads, head_conv=head_conv, NLayer1=4, NLayer2=4)
92
93
94	    # model = nn.DataParallel(model)
95	    print("Let's use", torch.cuda.device_count(), "GPUs!")
96	    if args.use_sgd:
97	        print("Use SGD")
98	        opt = optim.Adam(model.parameters(), lr=args.lr, weight_decay=1e-4)
99	        # opt = optim.SGD(model.parameters(), lr=args.lr, momentum=args.momentum, weight_decay=1e-4)
100	    else:
101	        print("Use Adam")
102	        opt = optim.Adam(model.parameters(), lr=args.lr, weight_decay=1e-4)
103
104	    if args.scheduler == 'cos':
105	        scheduler = CosineAnnealingLR(opt, args.epochs, eta_min=0.5e-6, last_epoch=-1)
106	    elif args.scheduler == 'step':
107	        scheduler = StepLR(opt, step_size=20, gamma=0.7)
108
109
110	    model.cuda()
111	    model.train()
112	    io.cprint(
113	        f"Train knobs: img={cfg.IMG_Width}x{cfg.IMG_Height}, "
114	        f"heatmap_target={cfg.HEATMAP_TARGET}, rotation={cfg.ROTATION_DEGREES}, "
115	        f"color_aug={cfg.USE_COLOR_AUG}, target_mode={args.target_mode}, "
116	        f"observer_alpha={args.observer_alpha}, num_workers={args.num_workers}, "
117	        f"hcrn_v1={getattr(model, 'hcrn_v1', False)}"
118	    )
119	    if getattr(model, 'hcrn_v1', False):
120	        io.cprint(f"HCRN-v1 group_path={getattr(model, 'hcrn_v1_group_path', '')}")
121	        io.cprint(f"HCRN-v1 certain_idx={model.hcrn_v1_certain_idx.tolist()}")
122	        io.cprint(f"HCRN-v1 uncertain_idx={model.hcrn_v1_uncertain_idx.tolist()}")
123	    scaler = GradScaler()
124	    inter_nums = len(train_loader)
125	    total_acc = 0
126	    TMAXcounts = None
127	    for epoch in range(0, args.epochs):
128	        ####################
129	        # Train
130	        ####################
131
132	        train_loss = 0.0
133	        inint_loss = 0.0
134	        loss_ml = 0.0
135	        loss_dl = 0.0
136	        edgeloss = 0
137	        # for data, edges, label in train_loader:
138	        tic = time.time()
139	        nums = 0
140	        model.train()
141	        tic = time.time()
142	        for batch in train_loader:
143	            if args.target_mode == "mean":
144	                train_data, hotmap, hot_mapl, offestxy, mask_, label_re = batch
145	                observer_re = None
146	            else:
147	                train_data, hotmap, hot_mapl, offestxy, mask_, label_re, observer_re = batch
148	            train_data = train_data.cuda().float()
149	            hotmap = hotmap.cuda().float()
150	            hot_mapl = hot_mapl.cuda().float()
151	            offestxy = offestxy.cuda().float()
152	            mask_ = mask_.cuda().float()
153	            label_re = label_re.cuda().float()
154	            if observer_re is not None:
155	                observer_re = observer_re.cuda().float()
156
157	            nums = nums +1
158	            opt.zero_grad()
159	            with autocast():
160
161	                outputs, inint_coords, prehotmap = model(train_data)
162	                inint_loss_ = observer_aware_rle(model.Initloss, inint_coords, label_re,
163	                                                 observer_re, args.target_mode, args.observer_alpha)
164	                loss1 = observer_aware_rle(model.loss, outputs[0], label_re,
165	                                           observer_re, args.target_mode, args.observer_alpha)
166	                loss2 = observer_aware_rle(model.loss, outputs[1], label_re,
167	                                           observer_re, args.target_mode, args.observer_alpha)
168	                loss3 = observer_aware_rle(model.loss, outputs[2], label_re,
169	                                           observer_re, args.target_mode, args.observer_alpha)
170	                loss4 = observer_aware_rle(model.loss, outputs[3], label_re,
171	                                           observer_re, args.target_mode, args.observer_alpha)
172	                loss = loss1 + loss2 + loss3 + loss4
173
174	                loss_ml_, loss_dl_, loss_re_, loss_fl_ = rcal_loss(prehotmap, hot_mapl)
175	                edgeloss_ = loss_fl_  # edge_loss(outputs, label_re.repeat(1, 4, 1))
176
177	                loss = inint_loss_ + loss + loss_ml_ + loss_dl_  # + edgeloss_
178
179	                scaler.scale(loss).backward()
180	                # Unscales gradients and calls
181	                # or skips optimizer.step()
182	                scaler.step(opt)
183	                # Updates the scale for next iteration
184	                scaler.update()
185
186	            train_loss += loss.item()
187	            inint_loss += inint_loss_.item()
188	            loss_ml += loss_ml_.item()
189	            loss_dl += loss_dl_.item()
190	            edgeloss += edgeloss_.item()
191	            if nums % cfg.VIEW_NUMS == 0:
192	                toc = time.time()
193	                train_loss = train_loss/ (cfg.VIEW_NUMS)
194	                inint_loss = inint_loss/ (cfg.VIEW_NUMS)
195	                loss_ml = loss_ml/ (cfg.VIEW_NUMS)
196	                loss_dl = loss_dl/ (cfg.VIEW_NUMS)
197	                edgeloss = edgeloss/ (cfg.VIEW_NUMS)
198
199	                print("lr = ", opt.param_groups[0]['lr'], "loss1 = ", loss1.item(), "loss2 = ", loss2.item(), "loss3 = ", loss3.item(), "loss4 = ", loss4.item())
200	                outstr = 'epoch %d /%d,epoch %d /%d, loss: %.6f, inint_loss: %.6f, loss_ml: %.6f, loss_dl: %.6f, edgeloss: %.6f, const time: %.6f' % (
201	                 epoch,args.epochs, nums, inter_nums, train_loss, inint_loss, loss_ml, loss_dl, edgeloss, toc - tic)
202
203	                io.cprint(outstr)
204	                train_loss = 0.0
205	                inint_loss = 0.0
206	                loss_ml = 0.0
207	                loss_dl = 0.0
208	                edgeloss = 0.0
209	                tic = time.time()
210	        if 0 == epoch % 10 and epoch>=200:
211	            model.eval()
212	            num = 0
213	            total_masks = 0
214	            total_counts = []
215	            for rowImg, test_data, label_coords_, scalek, sizek in test_loader:
216	                test_data = test_data.cuda().float()
217	                # with autocast():
218	                scalek = scalek.squeeze().numpy()
219	                sizek = sizek.squeeze().numpy()
220	                with torch.no_grad():
221	                    outputs, inint_coords, hotmap = model(test_data)
222	                    pred = outputs[-1][:, :, :2]
223
224	                    key_points, mask_ = decode_reg(pred)
225	                    pcoords = key_points[:, 1:3] * scalek
226	                    offv = 300
227	                    x1, y1 = max(int(np.min(pcoords[:, 0])) - offv + 100, 0), max(int(np.min(pcoords[:, 1])) - offv, 0)
228	                    x2, y2 = int(np.max(pcoords[:, 0])) + offv + 100, int(np.max(pcoords[:, 1])) + offv
229	                    cropimg = torch.squeeze(rowImg)[y1:y2, x1:x2, :].numpy()
230	                    lheight, lwidth, _ = cropimg.shape
231	                    rowImg_ = np.copy(cropimg)
232	                    cropimg = cv2.resize(cropimg, (cfg.IMG_Width, cfg.IMG_Height), interpolation=cv2.INTER_LINEAR)
233	                    cropimg = cropimg / np.max(cropimg)
234	                    scalex = 1.0 * lwidth / cfg.IMG_Width
235	                    scaley = 1.0 * lheight / cfg.IMG_Height
236	                    scalek = np.array([[scalex, scaley]])
237	                    cropimg = torch.tensor(cropimg).unsqueeze(dim=0).permute(0, 3, 1, 2).cuda().float()
238
239	                    outputs, inint_coords, hotmap = model(cropimg)
240	                    pred = outputs[-1][:, :, :2]
241	                    key_points, mask_ = decode_reg(pred)
242	                    label_coords_ = label_coords_ - torch.tensor(np.array([[x1, y1]]))
243	                    #
244	                    label_coords_ = label_coords_.squeeze().numpy()
245	                    # rowImg = rowImg.squeeze().numpy()
246
247	                    counts, key_points = cal_acc(rowImg_, key_points, mask_, label_coords_, scalek)
248	                    total_counts.append(counts)
249	                    total_masks = total_masks + np.sum(mask_)
250	                    num = num + 1
251
252	            total_counts = np.array(total_counts)
253	            TWOMM = np.sum(total_counts < cfg.ERROR_RANGE[0], axis=0)
254	            print(TWOMM / num)
255	            total_points = num * cfg.PointNms
256	            print("total_points = ", total_points, "     total_masks = ", total_masks)
257	            print("2mm  acc = ", np.sum(total_counts < cfg.ERROR_RANGE[0]) / total_points)
258	            print("2.5mm  acc = ", np.sum(total_counts < cfg.ERROR_RANGE[1]) / total_points)
259	            print("3mm  acc = ", np.sum(total_counts < cfg.ERROR_RANGE[2]) / total_points)
260	            print("4mm  acc = ", np.sum(total_counts < cfg.ERROR_RANGE[3]) / total_points)

293	    torch.backends.cudnn.enabled = True
294	    # Training settings
295	    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description='Point Cloud Recognition')
296	    parser.add_argument('--exp_name', type=str, default='cls_1024', metavar='N',
297	                        help='Name of the experiment')
298	    parser.add_argument('--model', type=str, default='dgcnn', metavar='N',
299	                        choices=['pointnet', 'dgcnn'],
300	                        help='Model to use, [pointnet, dgcnn]')
301	    parser.add_argument('--dataset', type=str, default='modelnet40', metavar='N',
302	                        choices=['modelnet40'])
303	    parser.add_argument('--batch_size', type=int, default=5, metavar='batch_size',
304	                        help='Size of batch)')
305	    parser.add_argument('--test_batch_size', type=int, default=1, metavar='batch_size',
306	                        help='Size of batch)')
307	    parser.add_argument('--epochs', type=int, default=1001, metavar='N',
308	                        help='number of episode to train ')
309	    parser.add_argument('--use_sgd', type=bool, default=True,
310	                        help='Use SGD')#0.2*1e-3
311	    parser.add_argument('--lr', type=float, default= 0.2*1e-3, metavar='LR',
312	                        help='learning rate (default: 0.001, 0.1 if using sgd)')
313	    parser.add_argument('--momentum', type=float, default=0.9, metavar='M',
314	                        help='SGD momentum (default: 0.9)')
315	    parser.add_argument('--scheduler', type=str, default='cos', metavar='N',
316	                        choices=['cos', 'step'],
317	                        help='Scheduler to use, [cos, step]')
318	    parser.add_argument('--no_cuda', type=bool, default=False,
319	                        help='enables CUDA training')
320	    parser.add_argument('--seed', type=int, default=42, metavar='S',
321	                        help='random seed (default: 1)')
322	    parser.add_argument('--eval', type=bool, default=False,
323	                        help='evaluate the model')
324	    parser.add_argument('--num_points', type=int, default=2048,
325	                        help='num of points to use')
326	    parser.add_argument('--dropout', type=float, default=0.5,
327	                        help='initial dropout rate')
328	    parser.add_argument('--emb_dims', type=int, default=2048, metavar='N',
329	                        help='Dimension of embeddings')
330	    parser.add_argument('--k', type=int, default=40, metavar='N',
331	                        help='Num of nearest neighbors to use')
332	    parser.add_argument('--model_path', type=str, default='', metavar='N',
333	                        help='Pretrained model path')
334	    parser.add_argument('--target_mode', type=str, default='mean',
335	                        choices=['mean', 'observer_avg_nll', 'observer_mixed_nll'],
336	                        help='Target supervision mode for DuoAnno experiments')
337	    parser.add_argument('--observer_alpha', type=float, default=0.5,
338	                        help='Observer loss weight for observer_mixed_nll')
339	    parser.add_argument('--num_workers', type=int, default=0,
340	                        help='DataLoader workers for training')
341	    parser.add_argument('--limit_train_samples', type=int, default=0,
342	                        help='Limit training samples for overfit/smoke tests; 0 uses all data')
343	    parser.add_argument('--hcrn_v1', action='store_true',
344	                        default=os.environ.get('DELR_HCRN_V1', '0') == '1',
345	                        help='Enable true two-stage HCRN-v1')
346	    parser.add_argument('--hcrn_group_path', type=str, default=os.environ.get('DELR_HCRN_GROUP_PATH', ''),
347	                        help='Optional train-only HCRN group json path')
348	    args = parser.parse_args()
349	    os.environ['DELR_HCRN_V1'] = '1' if args.hcrn_v1 else '0'
350	    if args.hcrn_group_path:
351	        os.environ['DELR_HCRN_GROUP_PATH'] = args.hcrn_group_path
352
353	    _init_()
354
355	    io = IOStream('outputs/' + args.exp_name + '/run.log')
356	    io.cprint(str(args))
357
358	    args.cuda = not args.no_cuda and torch.cuda.is_available()
359	    torch.manual_seed(args.seed)
360	    np.random.seed(args.seed)
361	    if args.cuda:
362	        io.cprint(
363	            'Using GPU : ' + str(torch.cuda.current_device()) + ' from ' + str(torch.cuda.device_count()) + ' devices')
364	        torch.cuda.manual_seed(args.seed)
365	    else:
366	        io.cprint('Using CPU')
367
368	    if not args.eval:
369	        train(args, io)

18	ISBI2015_ROOT = os.environ.get("ISBI2015_ROOT", "/root/autodl-tmp/D-CeLR-master/data3/ISBI2015")
19	TEST_SPLIT = os.environ.get("ISBI2015_TEST_SPLIT", "Test1Data")
20	TEST1_IMG_DIR = os.path.join(ISBI2015_ROOT, "RawImage", TEST_SPLIT)
21	ANNOTATION_DIR = os.path.join(ISBI2015_ROOT, "AnnotationsByMD")
22	DEFAULT_MODEL_PATH = os.environ.get("DELR_MODEL_PATH", "./outputs/best.pth")
23
24
25	def resolve_model_path():
26	    preferred = Path(DEFAULT_MODEL_PATH)
27	    if preferred.exists():
28	        return str(preferred)
29
30	    output_dir = Path("./outputs")
31	    checkpoints = sorted(output_dir.glob("**/ceph_model_*.pth"))
32	    if checkpoints:
33	        return str(checkpoints[-1])
34
35	    raise FileNotFoundError(
36	        f"No checkpoint found. Checked '{preferred}' and '{output_dir / 'ceph_model_*.pth'}'."
37	    )
38
39
40
41	def model_initial(model, model_name):
42	    # 加载预训练模型
43	    pretrained_dict = torch.load(model_name)["model"]
44	    model_dict = model.state_dict()
45	    # 1. filter out unnecessary keys
46	    pretrained_dictf = {k: v for k, v in pretrained_dict.items() if k in model_dict}
47	    # 2. overwrite entries in the existing state dict
48	    model_dict.update(pretrained_dictf)
49	    # 3. load the new state dict
50	    model.load_state_dict(model_dict)
51
52	    return model
53
54
