from net.ceph_reg_refine_net import get_model
import config.config as cfg

ISBI2015_ROOT = os.environ.get("ISBI2015_ROOT", "/root/autodl-tmp/D-CeLR-master/data3/ISBI2015")
TEST_SPLIT = os.environ.get("ISBI2015_TEST_SPLIT", "Test1Data")
TEST1_IMG_DIR = os.path.join(ISBI2015_ROOT, "RawImage", TEST_SPLIT)
ANNOTATION_DIR = os.path.join(ISBI2015_ROOT, "AnnotationsByMD")
DEFAULT_MODEL_PATH = os.environ.get("DELR_MODEL_PATH", "./outputs/best.pth")

def resolve_model_path():
preferred = Path(DEFAULT_MODEL_PATH)
if preferred.exists():
return str(preferred)

output_dir = Path("./outputs")
checkpoints = sorted(output_dir.glob("**/ceph_model_*.pth"))
if checkpoints:
return str(checkpoints[-1])

raise FileNotFoundError(
f"No checkpoint found. Checked '{preferred}' and '{output_dir / 'ceph_model_*.pth'}'."
)

def model_initial(model, model_name):
ckpt = torch.load(model_name, map_location="cpu")
pretrained_dict = ckpt["model"]
model_keys = set(model.state_dict().keys())
ckpt_keys = set(pretrained_dict.keys())

model_has_hcrn = any(k.startswith("hcrn_v2_") for k in model_keys)
ckpt_has_hcrn = any(k.startswith("hcrn_v2_") for k in ckpt_keys)

if model_has_hcrn and not ckpt_has_hcrn:
raise RuntimeError(
"DELR_HCRN_V2=1 built an HCRN-v2 model, but the checkpoint has no "
"hcrn_v2_* parameters. Do not evaluate a plain DELR checkpoint as HCRN-v2."
)
if ckpt_has_hcrn and not model_has_hcrn:
raise RuntimeError(
"Checkpoint contains hcrn_v2_* parameters, but DELR_HCRN_V2 is not enabled. "
"Set DELR_HCRN_V2=1 before evaluation."
)

result = model.load_state_dict(pretrained_dict, strict=False)
print("Missing keys:", result.missing_keys)
print("Unexpected keys:", result.unexpected_keys)

if model_has_hcrn:
missing_hcrn = [k for k in result.missing_keys if k.startswith("hcrn_v2_")]
unexpected_hcrn = [k for k in result.unexpected_keys if k.startswith("hcrn_v2_")]
if missing_hcrn or unexpected_hcrn:
raise RuntimeError(
f"HCRN-v2 checkpoint mismatch. missing={missing_hcrn}, "
f"unexpected={unexpected_hcrn}"
)

return model

546	    def _get_clones(self, module, N):
547	        return nn.ModuleList([copy.deepcopy(module) for i in range(N)])
548
549	    def _hcrn_v2_directed_conditioning(self, lm_tokens, reference_points, layer_idx):
550	        """Condition uncertain landmark tokens on certain tokens plus explicit coords."""
551	        if not self.hcrn_v2:
552	            return lm_tokens
553
554	        certain_idx = self.hcrn_v2_certain_idx.to(lm_tokens.device)
555	        uncertain_idx = self.hcrn_v2_uncertain_idx.to(lm_tokens.device)
556
557	        lm_certain = torch.index_select(lm_tokens, 1, certain_idx)
558	        lm_uncertain = torch.index_select(lm_tokens, 1, uncertain_idx)
559
560	        coords = reference_points.detach().clamp(0, 1)
561	        coords_certain = torch.index_select(coords, 1, certain_idx).to(lm_tokens.dtype)
562	        coords_uncertain = torch.index_select(coords, 1, uncertain_idx).to(lm_tokens.dtype)
563
564	        certain_kv = lm_certain + self.hcrn_v2_coord_pe(coords_certain)
565	        uncertain_q = lm_uncertain + self.hcrn_v2_coord_pe(coords_uncertain)
566	        certain_kv = self.hcrn_v2_kv_norms[layer_idx](certain_kv)
567	        uncertain_q = self.hcrn_v2_q_norms[layer_idx](uncertain_q)
568
569	        cond, attn = self.hcrn_v2_cross_attn[layer_idx](
570	            query=uncertain_q,
571	            key=certain_kv,
572	            value=certain_kv,
573	            need_weights=True,
574	            average_attn_weights=True,
575	        )
576	        if self.hcrn_v2_last_attn is None:
577	            self.hcrn_v2_last_attn = [None for _ in range(self.NLayer)]
578	        self.hcrn_v2_last_attn[layer_idx] = attn.detach()
579
580	        update = self.hcrn_v2_update_proj[layer_idx](cond)
581	        gate = 0.1 * torch.tanh(self.hcrn_v2_gates[layer_idx]).to(lm_tokens.dtype)
582	        lm_uncertain = lm_uncertain + gate * update
583
584	        return lm_tokens.index_copy(1, uncertain_idx, lm_uncertain)
585
586
587	    def _init_weights(self, m):
588	        if isinstance(m, nn.Linear):
589	            # we use xavier_uniform following official JAX ViT:
590	            torch.nn.init.xavier_uniform_(m.weight)
591	            if isinstance(m, nn.Linear) and m.bias is not None:
592	                nn.init.constant_(m.bias, 0)
593	        elif isinstance(m, nn.LayerNorm):
594	            nn.init.constant_(m.bias, 0)
595	            nn.init.constant_(m.weight, 1.0)
596

1	import json

6	os.environ["DELR_HCRN_V2"] = "1"
7	os.environ.setdefault("DELR_IMG_SIZE", "256")

9	from net.ceph_reg_refine_net import get_model  # noqa: E402

11
12	def build_model():
13	    return get_model(
14	        num_layers=34,
15	        heads={"hm": 1, "class": 19},
16	        head_conv=256,
17	        NLayer1=4,
18	        NLayer2=4,
19	    ).cuda()
20
21
22	def assert_close(name, value, threshold):
23	    if value > threshold:
24	        raise AssertionError(f"{name}={value} > {threshold}")
25
26
27	def grad_norm(params):
28	    total = 0.0
29	    for p in params:
30	        if p.grad is not None:
31	            total += float(p.grad.detach().float().norm().item())
32	    return total
33
34
35	def main():
36	    torch.manual_seed(42)
37	    summary = {}
38
39	    model = build_model().eval()
40	    summary["hcrn_v2_enabled"] = bool(model.hcrn_v2)
41	    summary["certain_idx"] = model.hcrn_v2_certain_idx.cpu().tolist()
42	    summary["uncertain_idx"] = model.hcrn_v2_uncertain_idx.cpu().tolist()
43	    summary["group_is_permutation"] = sorted(
44	        summary["certain_idx"] + summary["uncertain_idx"]
45	    ) == list(range(19))
46	    summary["num_certain"] = len(summary["certain_idx"])
47	    summary["num_uncertain"] = len(summary["uncertain_idx"])
48
49	    x = torch.randn(2, 3, int(os.environ["DELR_IMG_SIZE"]), int(os.environ["DELR_IMG_SIZE"]), device="cuda")
50	    with torch.no_grad():
51	        outputs, output1, hotmap = model(x)
52
53	    summary["len_outputs"] = len(outputs)
54	    summary["output_shape"] = list(outputs[-1].shape)
55	    summary["output1_shape"] = list(output1.shape)
56	    summary["hotmap_shape"] = list(hotmap.shape)
57	    summary["finite_outputs"] = bool(torch.isfinite(outputs[-1]).all().item())
58	    summary["finite_output1"] = bool(torch.isfinite(output1).all().item())
59	    summary["finite_hotmap"] = bool(torch.isfinite(hotmap).all().item())
60	    summary["attn_shapes"] = [
61	        list(a.shape) if a is not None else None for a in model.hcrn_v2_last_attn
62	    ]
63	    bounded_gates = 0.1 * torch.tanh(model.hcrn_v2_gates.detach())
64	    summary["initial_gates_raw"] = model.hcrn_v2_gates.detach().cpu().tolist()
65	    summary["initial_gates_bounded"] = bounded_gates.cpu().tolist()
66
67	    # Identity-init check: identical weights, one model with HCRN-v2 disabled,
68	    # one with HCRN-v2 enabled and zero gates.
69	    os.environ["DELR_HCRN_V2"] = "0"
70	    model_base = build_model().eval()
71	    os.environ["DELR_HCRN_V2"] = "1"
72	    model_hcrn = build_model().eval()
73	    model_hcrn.load_state_dict(model_base.state_dict(), strict=False)
74	    model_hcrn.hcrn_v2_gates.data.zero_()
75	    with torch.no_grad():
76	        out_base = model_base(x)[0][-1]
77	        out_hcrn = model_hcrn(x)[0][-1]
78	    identity_diff = (out_base - out_hcrn).abs().max().item()
79	    summary["identity_max_diff"] = identity_diff
80
81	    # Gate grad should be non-zero at zero gate.
82	    model_hcrn.train()
83	    model_hcrn.zero_grad(set_to_none=True)
84	    outputs, _output1, _hotmap = model_hcrn(x)
85	    loss = outputs[-1][:, :, :2].sum()
86	    loss.backward()
87	    summary["gate_grad_norm_at_zero_gate"] = grad_norm([model_hcrn.hcrn_v2_gates])
88	    adapter_params = []
89	    for modules in [
90	        model_hcrn.hcrn_v2_coord_pe,
91	        model_hcrn.hcrn_v2_q_norms,
92	        model_hcrn.hcrn_v2_kv_norms,
93	        model_hcrn.hcrn_v2_cross_attn,
94	        model_hcrn.hcrn_v2_update_proj,
95	    ]:
96	        adapter_params.extend(list(modules.parameters()))
97	    summary["adapter_grad_norm_at_zero_gate"] = grad_norm(adapter_params)
98
99	    # Once gate is non-zero, adapter internals should get gradients.
100	    model_hcrn.zero_grad(set_to_none=True)
101	    model_hcrn.hcrn_v2_gates.data.fill_(0.01)
102	    outputs, _output1, _hotmap = model_hcrn(x)
103	    loss = outputs[-1][:, :, :2].sum()
104	    loss.backward()
105	    summary["adapter_grad_norm_at_nonzero_gate"] = grad_norm(adapter_params)
106
107	    summary["overall_pass"] = all(
108	        [
109	            summary["hcrn_v2_enabled"],
110	            summary["group_is_permutation"],
111	            summary["num_certain"] == 10,
112	            summary["num_uncertain"] == 9,
113	            summary["len_outputs"] == 4,
114	            summary["output_shape"] == [2, 19, 4],
115	            summary["output1_shape"] == [2, 19, 4],
116	            summary["finite_outputs"],
117	            summary["finite_output1"],
118	            summary["finite_hotmap"],
119	            summary["attn_shapes"] == [[2, 9, 10]] * 4,
120	            abs(max(summary["initial_gates_bounded"], key=abs)) < 1e-12,
121	            identity_diff < 1e-7,
122	            summary["gate_grad_norm_at_zero_gate"] > 0,
123	            summary["adapter_grad_norm_at_zero_gate"] < 1e-10,
124	            summary["adapter_grad_norm_at_nonzero_gate"] > 0,
125	        ]
126	    )
127
128	    os.makedirs("outputs/hcrn_v2_sanity", exist_ok=True)
129	    with open("outputs/hcrn_v2_sanity/sanity_summary.json", "w") as f:
130	        json.dump(summary, f, indent=2)
131	    print(json.dumps(summary, indent=2))
132	    if not summary["overall_pass"]:
133	        raise SystemExit("SANITY_FAIL")
134	    print("SANITY_PASS")
135
136
137	if __name__ == "__main__":
138	    main()

6	from net.ceph_reg_refine_net import get_model  # noqa: E402
7	from test_ceph2015 import model_initial  # noqa: E402
8
9
10	def build(enabled):
11	    os.environ["DELR_HCRN_V2"] = "1" if enabled else "0"
12	    return get_model(34, heads={"hm": 1, "class": 19}, head_conv=256)
13
14
15	def main():
16	    os.makedirs("outputs/hcrn_v2_ckpt_guard", exist_ok=True)
17	    hcrn_path = "outputs/hcrn_v2_ckpt_guard/hcrn_v2_dummy_256.pth"
18	    plain_path = "outputs/hcrn_v2_ckpt_guard/plain_dummy_256.pth"
19	    torch.save({"model": build(True).state_dict(), "epoch": 0}, hcrn_path)
20	    torch.save({"model": build(False).state_dict(), "epoch": 0}, plain_path)
21
22	    checks = []
23
24	    try:
25	        model_initial(build(False), hcrn_path)
26	        checks.append(("hcrn_ckpt_into_plain", False, "unexpected pass"))
27	    except RuntimeError as exc:
28	        checks.append((
29	            "hcrn_ckpt_into_plain",
30	            "Set DELR_HCRN_V2=1" in str(exc),
31	            str(exc).split("\n")[0],
32	        ))
33
34	    try:
35	        model_initial(build(True), plain_path)
36	        checks.append(("plain_ckpt_into_hcrn", False, "unexpected pass"))
37	    except RuntimeError as exc:
38	        checks.append((
39	            "plain_ckpt_into_hcrn",
40	            "checkpoint has no hcrn_v2" in str(exc),
41	            str(exc).split("\n")[0],
42	        ))
43
44	    try:
45	        model_initial(build(True), hcrn_path)
46	        checks.append(("hcrn_ckpt_into_hcrn", True, "pass"))
47	    except Exception as exc:
48	        checks.append(("hcrn_ckpt_into_hcrn", False, str(exc).split("\n")[0]))
49
50	    for name, ok, msg in checks:
51	        print(f"{name}: {'PASS' if ok else 'FAIL'} | {msg}")
52	    if not all(ok for _, ok, _ in checks):
53	        raise SystemExit("CHECKPOINT_GUARD_FAIL")
54	    print("CHECKPOINT_GUARD_PASS")
55
56
57	if __name__ == "__main__":
58	    main()

+def _load_hcrn_v2_groups(num_landmarks):
+    """Load train-only disagreement groups for HCRN-v2 directed conditioning."""
+    default_certain = [11, 10, 8, 0, 6, 7, 1, 16, 13, 14]
+    default_uncertain = [17, 18, 12, 5, 2, 4, 3, 9, 15]
+    group_path = os.environ.get("DELR_HCRN_GROUP_PATH", "")
+
+    if group_path:
+        with open(group_path, "r") as f:
+            data = json.load(f)
+        certain = (
+            data.get("certain_idx")
+            or data.get("certain_indices")
+            or data.get("certain")
+        )
+        uncertain = (
+            data.get("uncertain_idx")
+            or data.get("uncertain_indices")
+            or data.get("uncertain")
+        )
+        if certain is None or uncertain is None:
+            raise ValueError(
+                "HCRN group JSON must contain certain_idx/certain_indices and "
+                "uncertain_idx/uncertain_indices."
+            )
+    else:
+        certain = default_certain
+        uncertain = default_uncertain
+
+    certain = [int(x) for x in certain]
+    uncertain = [int(x) for x in uncertain]
+    merged = sorted(certain + uncertain)
+    if merged != list(range(num_landmarks)):
+        raise ValueError(
+            f"HCRN groups must be a permutation of 0..{num_landmarks - 1}; "
+            f"got certain={certain}, uncertain={uncertain}"
+        )
+    return certain, uncertain, group_path
+

encoding.requires_grad = False

+        self.hcrn_v2 = os.environ.get("DELR_HCRN_V2", "0") == "1"
+        if self.hcrn_v2:
+            certain_idx, uncertain_idx, group_path = _load_hcrn_v2_groups(self.n_landmarks)
+            self.hcrn_v2_group_path = group_path
+            self.register_buffer(
+                "hcrn_v2_certain_idx",
+                torch.tensor(certain_idx, dtype=torch.long),
+            )
+            self.register_buffer(
+                "hcrn_v2_uncertain_idx",
+                torch.tensor(uncertain_idx, dtype=torch.long),
+            )
+            self.hcrn_v2_coord_pe = nn.Sequential(
+                nn.Linear(2, numchannel),
+                nn.GELU(),
+                nn.Linear(numchannel, numchannel),
+            )
+            self.hcrn_v2_q_norms = nn.ModuleList([
+                norm_layer(numchannel) for _ in range(self.NLayer)
+            ])
+            self.hcrn_v2_kv_norms = nn.ModuleList([
+                norm_layer(numchannel) for _ in range(self.NLayer)
+            ])
+            self.hcrn_v2_cross_attn = nn.ModuleList([
+                nn.MultiheadAttention(
+                    numchannel,
+                    numchannel // 64,
+                    batch_first=True,
+                    bias=True,
+                )
+                for _ in range(self.NLayer)
+            ])
+            self.hcrn_v2_update_proj = nn.ModuleList([
+                nn.Linear(numchannel, numchannel) for _ in range(self.NLayer)
+            ])
+            # Identity-init: gate=0 makes HCRN-v2 exactly the original DuoAnno-DELR path.
+            self.hcrn_v2_gates = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(self.NLayer), requires_grad=True)
+            self.hcrn_v2_last_attn = None
+        else:
+            self.hcrn_v2_group_path = ""
+            self.hcrn_v2_last_attn = None
+

@@ -464,6 +546,43 @@
def _get_clones(self, module, N):
return nn.ModuleList([copy.deepcopy(module) for i in range(N)])

+    def _hcrn_v2_directed_conditioning(self, lm_tokens, reference_points, layer_idx):
+        """Condition uncertain landmark tokens on certain tokens plus explicit coords."""
+        if not self.hcrn_v2:
+            return lm_tokens
+
+        certain_idx = self.hcrn_v2_certain_idx.to(lm_tokens.device)
+        uncertain_idx = self.hcrn_v2_uncertain_idx.to(lm_tokens.device)
+
+        lm_certain = torch.index_select(lm_tokens, 1, certain_idx)
+        lm_uncertain = torch.index_select(lm_tokens, 1, uncertain_idx)
+
+        coords = reference_points.detach().clamp(0, 1)
+        coords_certain = torch.index_select(coords, 1, certain_idx).to(lm_tokens.dtype)
+        coords_uncertain = torch.index_select(coords, 1, uncertain_idx).to(lm_tokens.dtype)
+
+        certain_kv = lm_certain + self.hcrn_v2_coord_pe(coords_certain)
+        uncertain_q = lm_uncertain + self.hcrn_v2_coord_pe(coords_uncertain)
+        certain_kv = self.hcrn_v2_kv_norms[layer_idx](certain_kv)
+        uncertain_q = self.hcrn_v2_q_norms[layer_idx](uncertain_q)
+
+        cond, attn = self.hcrn_v2_cross_attn[layer_idx](
+            query=uncertain_q,
+            key=certain_kv,
+            value=certain_kv,
+            need_weights=True,
+            average_attn_weights=True,
+        )
+        if self.hcrn_v2_last_attn is None:
+            self.hcrn_v2_last_attn = [None for _ in range(self.NLayer)]
+        self.hcrn_v2_last_attn[layer_idx] = attn.detach()
+
+        update = self.hcrn_v2_update_proj[layer_idx](cond)
+        gate = 0.1 * torch.tanh(self.hcrn_v2_gates[layer_idx]).to(lm_tokens.dtype)
+        lm_uncertain = lm_uncertain + gate * update
+
+        return lm_tokens.index_copy(1, uncertain_idx, lm_uncertain)
+

def _init_weights(self, m):
if isinstance(m, nn.Linear):
@@ -476,6 +595,8 @@
nn.init.constant_(m.weight, 1.0)

+        if self.hcrn_v2:
+            self.hcrn_v2_last_attn = None
layer1, layer2, layer3, output = self.backone(x)
hotmap = self.out1(output)

+            "hcrn_v2_* parameters. Do not evaluate a plain DELR checkpoint as HCRN-v2."
+        )

+            "Set DELR_HCRN_V2=1 before evaluation."
+        )
+

+    print("Missing keys:", result.missing_keys)
+    print("Unexpected keys:", result.unexpected_keys)
+
+    if model_has_hcrn:
+        missing_hcrn = [k for k in result.missing_keys if k.startswith("hcrn_v2_")]
+        unexpected_hcrn = [k for k in result.unexpected_keys if k.startswith("hcrn_v2_")]
+        if missing_hcrn or unexpected_hcrn:
+            raise RuntimeError(
+                f"HCRN-v2 checkpoint mismatch. missing={missing_hcrn}, "
+                f"unexpected={unexpected_hcrn}"
+            )

330
331	    def _make_layer(self, block, planes, blocks, stride=1):
332	        downsample = None
333	        if stride != 1 or self.inplanes != planes * block.expansion:
334	            downsample = nn.Sequential(
335	                nn.Conv2d(self.inplanes, planes * block.expansion,
336	                          kernel_size=1, stride=stride, bias=False),
337	                nn.BatchNorm2d(planes * block.expansion, momentum=BN_MOMENTUM),
338	            )
339
340	        layers = []
341	        layers.append(block(self.inplanes, planes, stride, downsample))
342	        self.inplanes = planes * block.expansion
343	        for i in range(1, blocks):
344	            layers.append(block(self.inplanes, planes))
345
346	        return nn.Sequential(*layers)
347

350	    def forward(self, x):
351	        conv1 = self.conv1(x)
352	        conv1 = self.bn1(conv1)
353	        conv1 = self.relu(conv1)
354
355	        x = self.maxpool(conv1)
356
357	        layer1 = self.layer1(x)
358	        layer2 = self.layer2(layer1)
359	        layer3 = self.layer3(layer2)
360	        layer4 = self.layer4(layer3)
361
362
363
364	        return layer1, layer2, layer3, layer4

372	            print('=> init deconv weights from normal distribution')

376	    def __init__(self, in_channel, out_channel, bias=True, norm=True):
377	        super(Linear_with_norm, self).__init__()
378	        self.bias = bias

380	        self.linear = nn.Linear(in_channel, out_channel, bias)
381	        nn.init.xavier_uniform_(self.linear.weight, gain=0.01)

我审查了最新 `FIXED` 包。结论：**这版已经修掉了上次我指出的主要问题，可以进入 5-image overfit 和 100epoch pilot；但正式实验前还建议再补 2 个防呆。**

## 总体评级

```text
结构实现：通过
sanity 覆盖：基本通过
checkpoint 防呆：基本通过
训练日志：通过
正式实验可信度：接近通过，但建议再修 2 个小问题
```

这版比上一版明显更稳。

---

# 已修好的关键点

## 1. checkpoint guard 已经补上

`test_ceph2015.py` 现在会检查：

```python
model_has_hcrn = any(k.startswith("hcrn_v2_") for k in model_keys)
ckpt_has_hcrn = any(k.startswith("hcrn_v2_") for k in ckpt_keys)
```

并且会拦截两类危险情况：

```text
HCRN-v2 模型加载普通 DELR checkpoint：报错
普通 DELR 模型加载 HCRN-v2 checkpoint：报错
```

这修掉了我上次说的最大风险：**静默测错模型**。

---

## 2. sanity check 覆盖到核心风险

包里的 `sanity_summary.json` 显示：

```json
"attn_shapes": [[2, 9, 10], [2, 9, 10], [2, 9, 10], [2, 9, 10]],
"identity_max_diff": 0.0,
"gate_grad_norm_at_zero_gate": 0.10486199706792831,
"adapter_grad_norm_at_zero_gate": 0.0,
"adapter_grad_norm_at_nonzero_gate": 0.23978264732068055,
"overall_pass": true
```

这说明几个关键设计都成立：

```text
9 个 uncertain 点确实 attend 到 10 个 certain 点；
gate=0 时，HCRN-v2 与原 DELR 完全等价；
gate=0 时，gate 自身有梯度；
gate 非 0 后，adapter 内部参数有梯度；
attention shape 正确；
输出 shape 正确。
```

这部分现在是合格的。

---

## 3. gate 日志已经补上

`train_ceph2015.py` 每个 epoch 会打印：

```text
HCRN-v2 gates raw=[...] bounded=[...]
```

这个很重要。后面 pilot 结果不好时，至少能判断是：

```text
adapter 被 gate 关掉了；
还是 adapter 确实参与了但没有带来泛化提升。
```

---

## 4. v2 adapter 插入位置正确

核心逻辑还是正确的：

```python
xc_ = cpb(xc_)
lm_tokens = xc_[:, -self.n_landmarks:, :]
lm_tokens = self._hcrn_v2_directed_conditioning(lm_tokens, reference_points, i)
xc_ = torch.cat([xc_[:, :-self.n_landmarks, :], lm_tokens], dim=1)
tmp = self.fc_coord_branches[i](xc_[:, -self.n_landmarks:, :])
```

也就是：

```text
原 DELR block
→ HCRN-v2 directed conditioning
→ 坐标增量 head
```

这是我认为最合理的位置。

---

# 还需要修的两个问题

## 问题 1：`DELR_HCRN_GROUP_PATH` 可能残留环境变量

现在训练代码是：

```python
os.environ['DELR_HCRN_V2'] = '1' if args.hcrn_v2 else '0'
if args.hcrn_group_path:
os.environ['DELR_HCRN_GROUP_PATH'] = args.hcrn_group_path
```

问题是：
如果你之前 shell 里设置过 `DELR_HCRN_GROUP_PATH`，这次运行时没有传 `--hcrn_group_path`，旧环境变量仍然会生效。

这样你以为用的是默认 canonical group，实际可能用了上一次的 group json。

建议改成：

```python
os.environ['DELR_HCRN_V2'] = '1' if args.hcrn_v2 else '0'

if args.hcrn_group_path:
os.environ['DELR_HCRN_GROUP_PATH'] = args.hcrn_group_path
else:
os.environ.pop('DELR_HCRN_GROUP_PATH', None)
```

`sanity_check_hcrn_v2.py` 里也建议加：

```python
os.environ.pop("DELR_HCRN_GROUP_PATH", None)
```

除非你是专门测试自定义 group。

这个不是架构 bug，但会影响实验可复现性。

---

## 问题 2：`test_ceph2015.py` 对非 HCRN 参数仍然是 `strict=False`

现在是：

```python
result = model.load_state_dict(pretrained_dict, strict=False)
print("Missing keys:", result.missing_keys)
print("Unexpected keys:", result.unexpected_keys)
```

它只对 HCRN-v2 相关 missing/unexpected 报错。
这已经比上一版好很多，但正式评估时仍然有风险：如果普通 backbone / DELR 参数缺失，它只打印，不会中断。

建议正式版改成：

```python
result = model.load_state_dict(pretrained_dict, strict=False)

if result.missing_keys or result.unexpected_keys:
raise RuntimeError(
f"Checkpoint mismatch. missing={result.missing_keys}, "
f"unexpected={result.unexpected_keys}"
)
```

或者更简单：

```python
model.load_state_dict(pretrained_dict, strict=True)
```

前提是 checkpoint 和模型版本完全一致。

这个建议很重要，因为后面你要比较 `Test1/Test2`，不能让任何参数加载问题被忽略。

---

# 不是 bug，但论文表述要注意

v2 不是纯粹的“完全有向层级网络”。它是：

```text
DELR 原始 self-attention block
+
每层内部插入 uncertain→certain directed residual adapter
```

因为 `cpb(xc_)` 里所有 token 还是会先对称通信，所以论文里不能写成：

```text
完全替代 DELR 的对称 self-attention
```

更准确的表述是：

```text
在 DELR refinement block 内部插入基于 observer disagreement hierarchy 的有向条件残差路径。
```

这个说法更安全，也更符合代码。

---

# 可以进入下一步了吗？

可以。

我建议你现在按这个顺序跑：

```text
1. 先修 DELR_HCRN_GROUP_PATH 环境变量残留问题
2. test loader 改成 strict mismatch 报错
3. 5-image overfit
4. seed42 / 100epoch pilot
5. Test1/Test2 评估
6. 输出 certain/uncertain 分组 MRE
7. 输出 gate 曲线
8. 保存 attention 权重做定性分析
```

100epoch pilot 的判断标准：

```text
Test2 overall MRE 是否低于 v1 的 1.3861
Test2 uncertain MRE 是否低于 v1 的 2.0400
certain 组是否不明显退化
gates 是否明显远离 0
attention 是否不是均匀分布
```

## 最终意见

**最新代码可以继续实验。**

但我建议不要直接宣称“代码完全定稿”。
更准确的状态是：

```text
HCRN-v2 fixed 版：代码审查基本通过，可进入 pilot；
正式结果前还需补环境变量清理和 strict checkpoint loading。
```

这版已经比 v1 和上一版 v2 稳很多，值得跑 5-image overfit 和 100epoch。

---

## 2. 5-image Overfit

```bash

--batch_size 2 \
--num_workers 0 \
--seed 42
```

```text
outputs/hcrn_v2_overfit_5img_e101_img512_seed42/overfit_eval_train5_summary.json
```

| checkpoint | final err | certain err | uncertain err | reference err | RLE loss |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|

| epoch100 | 49.17 px | 48.09 px | 50.38 px | 68.80 px | -1.196 |

Judgment:

```text
5-image overfit: PASS
```

The model can learn; both certain and uncertain groups fit the 5-image subset.

Evaluation checkpoint:


Evaluation logs confirm:

```text

Missing keys: []
Unexpected keys: []
```

## 4. Overall Metrics

| split | MRE | SDR@2mm | SDR@2.5mm | SDR@3mm | SDR@4mm |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|
| Test1 | 1.0540 | 0.8768 | 0.9326 | 0.9526 | 0.9828 |
| Test2 | 1.3951 | 0.7642 | 0.8311 | 0.8832 | 0.9495 |

Comparison to HCRN-v1 100-epoch pilot:

| method | Test1 MRE | Test2 MRE |
|---|---:|---:|
| HCRN-v1 true two-stage | 1.0476 | 1.3861 |
| HCRN-v2 in-DELR directed | 1.0540 | 1.3951 |

HCRN-v2 is slightly worse than HCRN-v1 at 100 epochs.

---

## 5. Certain vs Uncertain Group MRE

Groups:

```text
certain_idx   = [11, 10, 8, 0, 6, 7, 1, 16, 13, 14]
uncertain_idx = [17, 18, 12, 5, 2, 4, 3, 9, 15]
```

| split | all MRE | certain MRE | uncertain MRE |
|---|---:|---:|---:|
| Test1 | 1.0540 | 0.7516 | 1.3899 |
| Test2 | 1.3951 | 0.8115 | 2.0435 |

Comparison to HCRN-v1:

| method | Test2 all | Test2 certain | Test2 uncertain |
|---|---:|---:|---:|
| HCRN-v1 | 1.3861 | 0.7976 | 2.0400 |
| HCRN-v2 | 1.3951 | 0.8115 | 2.0435 |

HCRN-v2 does not improve the target uncertain group.

---

## 6. Gates

Final gates from training log:

```text
raw=[-0.019239, -0.009443, 0.000816, -0.000453]
bounded=[-1.9237e-03, -9.4426e-04, 8.1619e-05, -4.5328e-05]
```

Interpretation:

- Gates are non-zero, so the adapter was not completely ignored.
- Magnitudes remain small, especially layers 2-3.
- Participation exists, but it did not produce Test2 improvement.

---

## 7. Judgment

```text
HCRN-v2 100-epoch pilot: NEGATIVE
```

Reason:

- Code is trainable and passes 5-image overfit.
- Adapter gates move away from zero.
- But Test2 overall and uncertain-group MRE do not improve.

Recommendation:

- Do not run 1000 epoch or 3-seed for this version.
- HCRN-v2 can be recorded as a negative architecture pilot.
- If continuing HCRN, it needs a stronger intervention than a small gated residual adapter, or group-specific loss/DisAug must be tested as separate v2-B/v2-C ablations.

**tool：**

All the files uploaded by the user have been fully loaded. Searching won't provide additional information.

我觉得：**100 epoch 不一定能证明“最终没效果”，但已经足够判断“这个 v2-A 版本没有明显早期提升信号”。**

换句话说：

```text
不能说：多跑一定没用。
可以说：当前结果不支持直接上 1000 epoch / 3 seed。
```

## 为什么 100 epoch 已经有参考价值

这次不是训练没动。5-image overfit 是过的，epoch100 时 final err 从 `861.37 px` 降到 `49.17 px`，certain 和 uncertain 都能拟合，说明代码可训练。fileciteturn4file0L35-L58

而 100epoch pilot 评估也不是测错模型，日志确认了：

```text
DELR_HCRN_V2=1
Missing keys: []
Unexpected keys: []
```

所以这个负结果不是因为 checkpoint 或开关错误。fileciteturn4file0L75-L84

关键是：它在目标指标上没有任何趋势。Test2 MRE 是 `1.3951`，比 v1 的 `1.3861` 还略差；Test2 uncertain MRE 是 `2.0435`，也没有低于 v1 的 `2.0400`。fileciteturn4file0L88-L116

---

## 多跑会不会突然有效？

**有可能，但概率不高。**

原因是 gate 最终非常小：

```text
bounded=[-1.9237e-03, -9.4426e-04, 8.1619e-05, -4.5328e-05]
```

这说明 adapter 不是完全没梯度，但模型基本只给了它极小的残差权重。fileciteturn4file0L120-L130

如果 100 epoch 后 gate 还是 `1e-3` 量级，继续跑到 1000 epoch 可能出现两种情况：

```text
情况 A：gate 慢慢长大，然后才有效；
情况 B：gate 一直很小，adapter 始终只是微扰。
```

从目前结果看，**情况 B 更像**。因为如果 directed adapter 是强有效结构，通常 100 epoch 至少应该在 uncertain group 上看到一点正向信号，而现在连 Test2 uncertain 都没有下降。

---

## 我建议不要直接跑 1000 epoch

更合理的是做一个中间判断：

```text
从 epoch100 继续到 epoch300，作为 continuation probe。
```

但不要把它当正式实验，只看三个东西：

```text
1. Test2 uncertain MRE 有没有明显低于 2.04
2. gate 是否从 1e-3 级别增长到至少 1e-2 级别
3. validation/Test1 是否出现稳定改善，而不是随机波动
```

如果 epoch300 还是：

```text
Test2 uncertain ≈ 2.04
Test2 all ≈ 1.39
gate 仍然 1e-3
```

那就基本可以停，不值得 1000 epoch。

---

## 我的判断

**当前 v2-A 不值得直接长跑。**

但如果你担心 100 epoch 太短，可以做一个低成本确认：

```text
HCRN-v2-A seed42：继续跑到 300 epoch
不要 3-seed
不要 1000 epoch
只看 gate 曲线 + Test2 uncertain
```

如果 300 epoch 有明显趋势，再考虑 1000。
如果 300 epoch 没趋势，结论就是：**小 gated directed residual adapter 太弱，单独加结构不够，下一步应该做 v2-B：group-specific loss，或者 v2-C：DisAug，而不是继续堆 epoch。**

---

51:def observer_aware_rle(loss_fn, output, mean_target, observer_target, target_mode, alpha):

64:        return observer_loss
65:    if target_mode == "observer_mixed_nll":
66:        return (1.0 - alpha) * mean_loss + alpha * observer_loss

self.linear11 = nn.Linear(numchannel, 256)
self.linear12 = nn.Linear(256, 4)

self.transblock = nn.ModuleList([
Block(dim=numchannel, num_heads=numchannel//64, mlp_ratio=2, qkv_bias=True, norm_layer=norm_layer)
for i in range(self.NLayer)])
# self.linear21 = nn.Linear(numchannel, 256)
# self.linear22 = nn.Linear(256, 4)

fc_coord_branch = []
for _ in range(2):
fc_coord_branch.append(nn.Linear(numchannel, numchannel))
fc_coord_branch.append(nn.ReLU())
fc_coord_branch.append(nn.Linear(numchannel, 2))
fc_coord_branch = nn.Sequential(*fc_coord_branch)
self.fc_coord_branches = self._get_clones(fc_coord_branch, self.NLayer)
self.fc_coord_output_branches = self._get_clones(fc_coord_branch, self.NLayer)

fc_sigma_branch = []
for _ in range(2):
fc_sigma_branch.append(nn.Linear(numchannel, numchannel))
fc_sigma_branch.append(Linear_with_norm(numchannel, 2, norm=False))
fc_sigma_branch = nn.Sequential(*fc_sigma_branch)
self.fc_sigma_branches = self._get_clones(fc_sigma_branch, self.NLayer)

self.hcrn_v2 = os.environ.get("DELR_HCRN_V2", "0") == "1"
if self.hcrn_v2:
certain_idx, uncertain_idx, group_path = _load_hcrn_v2_groups(self.n_landmarks)
self.hcrn_v2_group_path = group_path
self.register_buffer(
"hcrn_v2_certain_idx",
torch.tensor(certain_idx, dtype=torch.long),
)
self.register_buffer(
"hcrn_v2_uncertain_idx",
torch.tensor(uncertain_idx, dtype=torch.long),
)
self.hcrn_v2_coord_pe = nn.Sequential(
nn.Linear(2, numchannel),
nn.GELU(),
nn.Linear(numchannel, numchannel),
)
self.hcrn_v2_q_norms = nn.ModuleList([
norm_layer(numchannel) for _ in range(self.NLayer)
])
self.hcrn_v2_kv_norms = nn.ModuleList([
norm_layer(numchannel) for _ in range(self.NLayer)
])
self.hcrn_v2_cross_attn = nn.ModuleList([
nn.MultiheadAttention(
numchannel,
numchannel // 64,
batch_first=True,
bias=True,
)
for _ in range(self.NLayer)
])
self.hcrn_v2_update_proj = nn.ModuleList([
nn.Linear(numchannel, numchannel) for _ in range(self.NLayer)
])
# Identity-init: gate=0 makes HCRN-v2 exactly the original DuoAnno-DELR path.
self.hcrn_v2_gates = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(self.NLayer), requires_grad=True)
self.hcrn_v2_last_attn = None
else:
self.hcrn_v2_group_path = ""
self.hcrn_v2_last_attn = None

self.loss = RLELoss(use_target_weight=False,
size_average=True,
residual=True,
q_dis='laplace')
self.Initloss = RLELoss(use_target_weight=False,
size_average=True,
residual=True,
q_dis='laplace')
self.initialize_weights()

print("")

def initialize_weights(self):
# initialization
# initialize (and freeze) pos_embed by sin-cos embedding
pos_embed = get_2d_sincos_pos_embed(self.pos_embed.shape[-1], self.sizem, cls_token=False)
self.pos_embed.data.copy_(torch.from_numpy(pos_embed).float().unsqueeze(0))

pos_embedly1 = get_2d_sincos_pos_embed(self.pos_embedly1.shape[-1], self.sizem*8, cls_token=False)
pos_embedly1 = pos_embedly1.reshape(self.sizem[0]*8, self.sizem[1]*8, 64)
self.pos_embedly1.data.copy_(torch.from_numpy(pos_embedly1).float().unsqueeze(0))

pos_embedly2 = get_2d_sincos_pos_embed(self.pos_embedly2.shape[-1], self.sizem*4, cls_token=False)
pos_embedly2 = pos_embedly2.reshape(self.sizem[0] * 4, self.sizem[1] * 4, 128)
self.pos_embedly2.data.copy_(torch.from_numpy(pos_embedly2).float().unsqueeze(0))

pos_embedly3 = get_2d_sincos_pos_embed(self.pos_embedly3.shape[-1], self.sizem*2, cls_token=False)
pos_embedly3 = pos_embedly3.reshape(self.sizem[0] * 2, self.sizem[1] * 2, 256)
self.pos_embedly3.data.copy_(torch.from_numpy(pos_embedly3).float().unsqueeze(0))

device = torch.device("cuda")
pos_embed1 = PositionalEncoding(self.encoder_embed.shape[1], self.encoder_embed.shape[2], device)
self.encoder_embed.data.copy_(pos_embed1.float().unsqueeze(0))

def _get_clones(self, module, N):
return nn.ModuleList([copy.deepcopy(module) for i in range(N)])

def _hcrn_v2_directed_conditioning(self, lm_tokens, reference_points, layer_idx):
"""Condition uncertain landmark tokens on certain tokens plus explicit coords."""
if not self.hcrn_v2:
return lm_tokens

certain_idx = self.hcrn_v2_certain_idx.to(lm_tokens.device)
uncertain_idx = self.hcrn_v2_uncertain_idx.to(lm_tokens.device)

lm_certain = torch.index_select(lm_tokens, 1, certain_idx)
lm_uncertain = torch.index_select(lm_tokens, 1, uncertain_idx)

coords = reference_points.detach().clamp(0, 1)
coords_certain = torch.index_select(coords, 1, certain_idx).to(lm_tokens.dtype)
coords_uncertain = torch.index_select(coords, 1, uncertain_idx).to(lm_tokens.dtype)

certain_kv = lm_certain + self.hcrn_v2_coord_pe(coords_certain)
uncertain_q = lm_uncertain + self.hcrn_v2_coord_pe(coords_uncertain)
certain_kv = self.hcrn_v2_kv_norms[layer_idx](certain_kv)
uncertain_q = self.hcrn_v2_q_norms[layer_idx](uncertain_q)

cond, attn = self.hcrn_v2_cross_attn[layer_idx](
query=uncertain_q,
key=certain_kv,
value=certain_kv,
need_weights=True,
average_attn_weights=True,
)
if self.hcrn_v2_last_attn is None:
self.hcrn_v2_last_attn = [None for _ in range(self.NLayer)]
self.hcrn_v2_last_attn[layer_idx] = attn.detach()

update = self.hcrn_v2_update_proj[layer_idx](cond)
gate = 0.1 * torch.tanh(self.hcrn_v2_gates[layer_idx]).to(lm_tokens.dtype)
lm_uncertain = lm_uncertain + gate * update

return lm_tokens.index_copy(1, uncertain_idx, lm_uncertain)

def _init_weights(self, m):
if isinstance(m, nn.Linear):
# we use xavier_uniform following official JAX ViT:
torch.nn.init.xavier_uniform_(m.weight)
if isinstance(m, nn.Linear) and m.bias is not None:
nn.init.constant_(m.bias, 0)
elif isinstance(m, nn.LayerNorm):
nn.init.constant_(m.bias, 0)
nn.init.constant_(m.weight, 1.0)

def forward(self, x):
if self.hcrn_v2:
self.hcrn_v2_last_attn = None
layer1, layer2, layer3, output = self.backone(x)
hotmap = self.out1(output)

b, c, h, w = output.shape
pos1 = self.pos_embedly1.expand(b, -1, -1, -1).permute(0, 3, 1, 2)
pos2 = self.pos_embedly2.expand(b, -1, -1, -1).permute(0, 3, 1, 2)
pos3 = self.pos_embedly3.expand(b, -1, -1, -1).permute(0, 3, 1, 2)

layer1 = self.bn1(self.conv1(F.interpolate(layer1, (self.sizem[0], self.sizem[1])))).view(b, c, h* w).permute(0, 2, 1)
layer2 = self.bn2(self.conv2(F.interpolate(layer2, (self.sizem[0], self.sizem[1])))).view(b, c, h* w).permute(0, 2, 1)
layer3 = self.bn3(self.conv3(F.interpolate(layer3, (self.sizem[0], self.sizem[1])))).view(b, c, h* w).permute(0, 2, 1)

pos1 = self.conv4(F.interpolate(pos1, (self.sizem[0], self.sizem[1]))).view(b, c, h* w).permute(0, 2, 1)
pos2 = self.conv5(F.interpolate(pos2, (self.sizem[0], self.sizem[1]))).view(b, c, h* w).permute(0, 2, 1)
pos3 = self.conv6(F.interpolate(pos3, (self.sizem[0], self.sizem[1]))).view(b, c, h* w).permute(0, 2, 1)

layer1 = layer1 + pos1
layer2 = layer2 + pos2
layer3 = layer3 + pos3

x4 = output.view(b, c, h* w).permute(0, 2, 1)
sizes = [b, c, h, w]
#################################################################
inc = x4 + self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1)
inc = torch.cat([inc,  self.encoder_embed.expand(b, -1, -1)], dim=1)
pos = torch.cat([self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1), self.encoder_embed.expand(b, -1, -1)], dim=1)

xcs = []
for cpb in self.InitBlock:
inc = cpb(inc)
xcs.append(inc)
inc = inc+pos
output1 = self.linear12(F.relu(self.linear11(xcs[-1][:, -self.n_landmarks:, :])))
#################################################################

# xc = (x4 + self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1))
xc = (x4 + self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1))*self.wg[0] + layer1*self.wg[1] + layer2*self.wg[2] + layer3*self.wg[3]
# inint_coords = get_proposal_pos_embed(output1[:, :, :2].detach(), num_pos_feats=512, temperature=10000)
output = x4 + self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1)
inint_coords = get_cls_embed(layer1, layer2, layer3, output, output1[:, :, :2].detach(), sizes, self.wcl, self.n_landmarks)

encoder_embed = self.encoder_embed.expand(b, -1, -1)  + inint_coords * self.inintv
# pos = torch.cat([self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1),encoder_embed], dim=1)
# pos = torch.cat([self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1) * self.pg[0] + pos1 * self.pg[1] + pos2 * self.pg[2] + pos3 * self.pg[3], encoder_embed], dim=1)

hs = []
inter_references = []
xc_ = torch.cat([xc, encoder_embed], dim=1)
reference_points = output1[:, :, :2].detach().clip(0, 1)
init_reference = reference_points
for i, cpb in enumerate(self.transblock):
xc_ = cpb(xc_)
lm_tokens = xc_[:, -self.n_landmarks:, :]
lm_tokens = self._hcrn_v2_directed_conditioning(lm_tokens, reference_points, i)
xc_ = torch.cat([xc_[:, :-self.n_landmarks, :], lm_tokens], dim=1)
tmp = self.fc_coord_branches[i](xc_[:, -self.n_landmarks:, :])

new_reference_points = tmp + inverse_sigmoid(reference_points)
new_reference_points = new_reference_points.sigmoid()

reference_points = new_reference_points

inint_coords = get_cls_embed(layer1, layer2, layer3, output, new_reference_points.detach(), sizes, self.wcl, self.n_landmarks)
# inint_coords = get_proposal_pos_embed(new_reference_points.detach(), num_pos_feats=512, temperature=10000)
encoder_embed = self.encoder_embed.expand(b, -1, -1) + inint_coords * self.inintv
pos = torch.cat([self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1) * self.pg[0] + pos1 * self.pg[1] + pos2 * self.pg[2] + pos3 * self.pg[3], encoder_embed], dim=1)
xc_ = xc_ + pos

inter_references.append(reference_points)
hs.append(xc_[:, -self.n_landmarks:, :])
outputs = []
for lvl in range(len(inter_references)):
if lvl == 0:
reference = init_reference
else:
reference = inter_references[lvl - 1]
reference = inverse_sigmoid(reference)

tmp = self.fc_coord_branches[lvl](hs[lvl])
tmp = tmp + reference

outputs_sigma = self.fc_sigma_branches[lvl](hs[lvl])

outputs_coord = tmp.sigmoid()
delta_coord_output = self.fc_coord_output_branches[lvl](hs[lvl])
outputs_coord = (outputs_coord + delta_coord_output)

outputs_coord = torch.cat([outputs_coord, outputs_sigma], dim=-1)
self.f.flush()

def close(self):
self.f.close()

def observer_aware_rle(loss_fn, output, mean_target, observer_target, target_mode, alpha):
"""Mean-anchored dual-annotation RLE for DuoAnno second-model control."""
mean_loss = loss_fn(output, mean_target)
if target_mode == "mean":
return mean_loss
if observer_target is None:
raise ValueError("observer_target is required for observer-aware target modes")

observer_loss = 0.5 * (
loss_fn(output, observer_target[:, 0]) +
loss_fn(output, observer_target[:, 1])
)
if target_mode == "observer_avg_nll":
return observer_loss
if target_mode == "observer_mixed_nll":
return (1.0 - alpha) * mean_loss + alpha * observer_loss
raise ValueError(f"Unsupported target_mode: {target_mode}")

def train(args, io):

file_path = TRAIN_IMG_DIR
label_path = ANNOTATION_DIR

train_loader = DataLoader(TrainData(file_path, label_path, target_mode=args.target_mode),
num_workers=args.num_workers,
batch_size=args.batch_size, shuffle=True, drop_last=True)
file_path = TEST1_IMG_DIR
label_path = ANNOTATION_DIR
test_loader = DataLoader(TestData(file_path, label_path), num_workers=0,
batch_size=1, shuffle=False, drop_last=False)

# Try to load models
num_layers =34
head_conv = 256
heads = {'hm': 1, 'class': cfg.PointNms}
model = get_model(num_layers=num_layers, heads=heads, head_conv=head_conv, NLayer1=4, NLayer2=4)

# model = nn.DataParallel(model)
print("Let's use", torch.cuda.device_count(), "GPUs!")
if args.use_sgd:
print("Use SGD")
opt = optim.Adam(model.parameters(), lr=args.lr, weight_decay=1e-4)
# opt = optim.SGD(model.parameters(), lr=args.lr, momentum=args.momentum, weight_decay=1e-4)
else:
print("Use Adam")
opt = optim.Adam(model.parameters(), lr=args.lr, weight_decay=1e-4)

if args.scheduler == 'cos':
scheduler = CosineAnnealingLR(opt, args.epochs, eta_min=0.5e-6, last_epoch=-1)
elif args.scheduler == 'step':
scheduler = StepLR(opt, step_size=20, gamma=0.7)

model.cuda()
model.train()
io.cprint(
f"Train knobs: img={cfg.IMG_Width}x{cfg.IMG_Height}, "
f"heatmap_target={cfg.HEATMAP_TARGET}, rotation={cfg.ROTATION_DEGREES}, "

)

io.cprint(f"DELR_HCRN_V2={os.environ.get('DELR_HCRN_V2', '0')}")
scaler = GradScaler()
inter_nums = len(train_loader)
total_acc = 0

####################

####################

train_loss = 0.0

loss_ml = 0.0

edgeloss = 0
# for data, edges, label in train_loader:

if args.target_mode == "mean":
train_data, hotmap, hot_mapl, offestxy, mask_, label_re = batch
observer_re = None
else:

with autocast():

outputs, inint_coords, prehotmap = model(train_data)

scaler.scale(loss).backward()
# Unscales gradients and calls
# or skips optimizer.step()

# Updates the scale for next iteration

我这里已经形成一个判断：不要把下一版做成“大杂烩”。v2A 继续跑 300epoch 是诊断；代码侧应该并行做 2-3 个小分支，每个只改一个核心变量，这样负结果也能解释。

我觉得可以并行，但**改代码这条线不要继续围着 v2A 原样小修**。
v2A 到 300epoch 只是回答一个问题：**gate 会不会后期长起来**。代码侧应该做更主动的 v2B / v2C。

当前 v2A 的问题很清楚：100epoch 时 Test2 overall `1.3951`，Test2 uncertain `2.0435`，都没有比 v1 好；而且 gate 只有 `1e-3` 量级，说明 directed adapter 虽然参与了，但影响非常弱。fileciteturn4file0L88-L130

所以我建议你并行这样做：

```text
GPU 线：v2A 继续跑到 300epoch，只做诊断
代码线：做 v2B / v2C，不要等 v2A-300
```

---

# 我建议优先改 4 个地方

## 1. 先改 optimizer：给 HCRN adapter 更高 lr，并且 gate 不做 weight decay

这是最小、最值得先做的改动。

现在 gate 太小，不一定是结构没用，也可能是：

```text
HCRN 参数从 0 gate 开始；
第一阶段 adapter 内部几乎没梯度；
所有参数和 DELR 主干用同一个 lr；
weight decay 还会把 gate 往 0 拉。
```

所以先把 optimizer 改成参数组：

```python
hcrn_gate_params = []
hcrn_adapter_params = []
base_params = []

for name, p in model.named_parameters():
if not p.requires_grad:
continue
if name == "hcrn_v2_gates":
hcrn_gate_params.append(p)
elif name.startswith("hcrn_v2_"):
hcrn_adapter_params.append(p)
else:
base_params.append(p)

opt = optim.Adam([
{"params": base_params, "lr": args.lr, "weight_decay": 1e-4},
{"params": hcrn_adapter_params, "lr": args.lr * args.hcrn_lr_mult, "weight_decay": 0.0},
{"params": hcrn_gate_params, "lr": args.lr * args.hcrn_gate_lr_mult, "weight_decay": 0.0},
])
```

新增参数：

```python
parser.add_argument("--hcrn_lr_mult", type=float, default=5.0)
parser.add_argument("--hcrn_gate_lr_mult", type=float, default=10.0)
```

这个分支可以叫：

```text
v2A-lr
```

它仍然不改 loss、不改结构，只测试：**v2A 失败是不是因为 adapter 太弱、gate 长不起来。**

---

## 2. 加 group-specific loss：这是 v2B，最应该做

现在训练目标仍然是统一 `observer_alpha=0.50`，但你真正想改善的是 uncertain group。v2A 结果也证明 target uncertain 没有被拉下来。fileciteturn4file0L102-L116

Claude 原设想其实就是：

```text
certain alpha = 0.3
uncertain alpha = 0.7
```

并且 uncertain 应该被更强监督。fileciteturn4file11L15-L39

我建议代码里加一个 grouped loss，不要替换原函数，新增函数：

```python
def observer_aware_rle_grouped(
loss_fn,
output,
mean_target,
observer_target,
certain_idx,
uncertain_idx,
alpha_certain=0.3,
alpha_uncertain=0.7,
uncertain_weight=1.5,
):
out_c = output[:, certain_idx]
out_u = output[:, uncertain_idx]

mean_c = mean_target[:, certain_idx]
mean_u = mean_target[:, uncertain_idx]

obs_c = observer_target[:, :, certain_idx]
obs_u = observer_target[:, :, uncertain_idx]

loss_c = observer_aware_rle(
loss_fn, out_c, mean_c, obs_c,
target_mode="observer_mixed_nll",
alpha=alpha_certain,
)

loss_u = observer_aware_rle(
loss_fn, out_u, mean_u, obs_u,
target_mode="observer_mixed_nll",
alpha=alpha_uncertain,
)

nc = len(certain_idx)
nu = len(uncertain_idx)

return (nc * loss_c + uncertain_weight * nu * loss_u) / (
nc + uncertain_weight * nu
)
```

训练里加开关：

```python
parser.add_argument("--hcrn_group_loss", action="store_true")
parser.add_argument("--hcrn_alpha_certain", type=float, default=0.3)
parser.add_argument("--hcrn_alpha_uncertain", type=float, default=0.7)
parser.add_argument("--hcrn_uncertain_weight", type=float, default=1.5)
```

然后 loss 部分：

```python
if args.hcrn_v2 and args.hcrn_group_loss:
certain_idx = model.hcrn_v2_certain_idx.tolist()
uncertain_idx = model.hcrn_v2_uncertain_idx.tolist()

loss1 = observer_aware_rle_grouped(...)
loss2 = observer_aware_rle_grouped(...)
loss3 = observer_aware_rle_grouped(...)
loss4 = observer_aware_rle_grouped(...)
inint_loss_ = observer_aware_rle_grouped(...)
else:
loss1 = observer_aware_rle(...)
```

这个分支叫：

```text
v2B-group-loss
```

我认为它比继续改 adapter 更重要，因为当前分组 premise 是成立的，但训练目标没有充分利用这个 premise。原始分析里 certain/uncertain disagreement 差距非常大，说明这个分组不是随便分的。fileciteturn4file13L1-L16

---

## 3. 加 relative coordinate conditioning：这是 v2C

v2A 现在有 absolute coord PE：

```python
certain_kv = lm_certain + coord_pe(coords_certain)
uncertain_q = lm_uncertain + coord_pe(coords_uncertain)
```

这个比 v1 好，但还不够。因为 uncertain 点真正需要的是：

```text
我相对 certain 点在哪里？
我和 certain 点之间的几何关系是什么？
```

不是只知道各自的绝对坐标。

可以在 `_hcrn_v2_directed_conditioning` 里加一个 relation PE：

```python
# coords_uncertain: [B, Nu, 2]
# coords_certain:   [B, Nc, 2]
rel = coords_uncertain.unsqueeze(2) - coords_certain.unsqueeze(1)
dist = torch.norm(rel, dim=-1, keepdim=True)

rel_input = torch.cat(
[rel, rel.abs(), dist],
dim=-1
)  # [B, Nu, Nc, 5]

rel_feat = self.hcrn_v2_rel_pe[layer_idx](rel_input)  # [B, Nu, Nc, C]
rel_cond = (attn.unsqueeze(-1) * rel_feat).sum(dim=2)  # [B, Nu, C]

update = self.hcrn_v2_update_proj[layer_idx](cond + rel_cond)
```

初始化里加：

```python
self.hcrn_v2_rel_pe = nn.ModuleList([
nn.Sequential(
nn.Linear(5, numchannel),
nn.GELU(),
nn.Linear(numchannel, numchannel),
)
for _ in range(self.NLayer)
])
```

这个分支叫：

```text
v2C-relative-geo
```

它比单纯 absolute PE 更符合头影测量逻辑：不确定点不是孤立定位，而是根据稳定骨性/牙性点的位置关系推断。

---

## 4. 加 uncertain-specific coordinate residual head：这是更强干预

现在 adapter 改的是 landmark token，最后还要经过共享的 `fc_coord_branches` 才影响坐标。
如果 gate 小、共享 head 又偏向原 DELR 表示，HCRN 的影响会被稀释。

可以给 uncertain 点加一个小的专属 residual coord head：

初始化：

```python
self.hcrn_v2_uncertain_coord_heads = nn.ModuleList([
nn.Sequential(
nn.Linear(numchannel, numchannel),
nn.GELU(),
nn.Linear(numchannel, 2),
)
for _ in range(self.NLayer)
])

self.hcrn_v2_coord_gates = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(self.NLayer))
```

forward 里，在：

```python
tmp = self.fc_coord_branches[i](xc_[:, -self.n_landmarks:, :])
```

之后加：

```python
if self.hcrn_v2:
uncertain_idx = self.hcrn_v2_uncertain_idx.to(tmp.device)
lm_uncertain = torch.index_select(lm_tokens, 1, uncertain_idx)

delta_u = self.hcrn_v2_uncertain_coord_heads[i](lm_uncertain)
coord_gate = 0.05 * torch.tanh(self.hcrn_v2_coord_gates[i]).to(tmp.dtype)

tmp_u = torch.index_select(tmp, 1, uncertain_idx)
tmp_u = tmp_u + coord_gate * delta_u
tmp = tmp.index_copy(1, uncertain_idx, tmp_u)
```

这个分支不要和 v2B 一开始混在一起。它可以叫：

```text
v2D-uncertain-coord-residual
```

这是更强的结构改动，专门让 HCRN 对 uncertain 坐标产生直接影响。

---

# 我建议的并行实验路线

你现在可以这样安排：

## GPU 继续跑

```text
v2A seed42：100 → 300 epoch
```

只看：

```text
Test2 uncertain 是否从 2.0435 降下来
gate 是否从 1e-3 长到 1e-2 以上
```

如果 300epoch gate 仍然很小，v2A 可以彻底停。

---

## 代码并行做 3 个分支

优先顺序：

```text
第一优先：v2A-lr
第二优先：v2B-group-loss
第三优先：v2C-relative-geo
```

不要一口气合成：

```text
v2A-lr + group-loss + relative-geo + coord-residual
```

否则结果好坏都解释不了。

---

# 我个人最看好的组合

如果只让我选一个最可能出信号的版本，我会选：

```text
v2B = v2A + HCRN 参数更高 lr + group-specific loss
```

也就是：

```bash
python train_ceph2015.py \
--hcrn_v2 \
--hcrn_lr_mult 5 \
--hcrn_gate_lr_mult 10 \
--hcrn_group_loss \
--hcrn_alpha_certain 0.3 \
--hcrn_alpha_uncertain 0.7 \
--hcrn_uncertain_weight 1.5 \
--target_mode observer_mixed_nll \
--observer_alpha 0.50 \
--epochs 101 \
--seed 42
```

这里 `--observer_alpha 0.50` 只是兼容旧逻辑；真正 group loss 里用的是 `0.3/0.7`。

---

# 还要补一个日志

无论哪个分支，都加 attention entropy 日志。只看 gate 不够。

每个 epoch 打印：

```text
layer0 attention entropy
layer1 attention entropy
layer2 attention entropy
layer3 attention entropy
```

如果 attention 接近均匀，说明 directed attention 没学到解剖依赖。
如果 entropy 降了，但 Test2 uncertain 不降，说明模型学到了某种固定关联，但这个关联对泛化没帮助。

---

# 最终建议

你现在并行是对的，但路线应该是：

```text
v2A-300：验证“是不是 epoch 不够”
v2A-lr：验证“是不是 adapter 太弱”
v2B-group-loss：验证“是不是目标没有拉 uncertain”
v2C-relative-geo：验证“是不是几何条件不够显式”
```

我的判断：**最优先改 optimizer + group-specific loss**。
因为当前 v2A 最大的问题不是代码不能学，而是 HCRN 信号太弱、uncertain 监督也不够强。

---

# HCRN-v2 四个隔离分支代码复审说明

日期：2026-05-17

本次只做代码改动与静态语法检查，不运行 forward / sanity / 训练。背景中的 v2A-300 诊断训练不受影响。

## 基线来源

所有分支都基于已审查通过的 HCRN-v2 fixed 版：

`/raid5/xuhd/MRC/code_audit/delr_20260505/DELR/DeLr_hcrn_v2_in_delr_directed_20260517`

该基线已经具备：

- `DELR_HCRN_V2=1` 开关；
- uncertain→certain directed adapter；
- coordinate PE；
- checkpoint guard；
- group path 环境变量清理；
- gate 与 attention entropy 日志基础。

## 桌面复审包

每个分支目录都包含：

- `train_ceph2015.py`
- `ceph_reg_refine_net.py`
- `train_ceph2015.diff`
- `ceph_reg_refine_net.diff`
- `README_CHANGELOG.md`

位置：

- `HCRN-v2A-lr/`
- `HCRN-v2B-group-loss/`
- `HCRN-v2C-relative-geo/`
- `HCRN-v2D-uncertain-coord-residual/`

## 服务器隔离目录

已规划并同步到服务器的隔离目录：

- `/raid5/xuhd/MRC/code_audit/delr_20260505/DELR/DeLr_hcrn_v2A_lr_20260517`
- `/raid5/xuhd/MRC/code_audit/delr_20260505/DELR/DeLr_hcrn_v2B_group_loss_20260517`
- `/raid5/xuhd/MRC/code_audit/delr_20260505/DELR/DeLr_hcrn_v2C_relative_geo_20260517`
- `/raid5/xuhd/MRC/code_audit/delr_20260505/DELR/DeLr_hcrn_v2D_uncertain_coord_residual_20260517`

## 分支意图

### v2A-lr

只改 optimizer，不改结构、不改 loss。

目的：验证 HCRN gate 太小是否因为 adapter 学习率太弱、gate 被 weight decay 拉回 0。

### v2B-group-loss

在 v2A-lr 基础上加 group-specific DuoAnno loss。

目的：验证 uncertain group 是否需要更强双标注监督和更高 loss 权重。

### v2C-relative-geo

在 v2A-lr 基础上加 uncertain-certain 相对几何编码。

目的：验证 absolute coordinate PE 不够时，显式相对几何是否能增强 directed conditioning。

### v2D-uncertain-coord-residual

在 v2A-lr 基础上给 uncertain 点增加专属坐标残差头。

目的：验证 HCRN adapter 影响被共享 coordinate head 稀释时，直接坐标残差是否能放大 uncertain 点更新。

## 静态检查

已通过：

```bash
python3 -m py_compile \
HCRN-v2A-lr/train_ceph2015.py HCRN-v2A-lr/ceph_reg_refine_net.py \
HCRN-v2B-group-loss/train_ceph2015.py HCRN-v2B-group-loss/ceph_reg_refine_net.py \
HCRN-v2C-relative-geo/train_ceph2015.py HCRN-v2C-relative-geo/ceph_reg_refine_net.py \
HCRN-v2D-uncertain-coord-residual/train_ceph2015.py HCRN-v2D-uncertain-coord-residual/ceph_reg_refine_net.py
```

未执行：

- 未跑训练；
- 未跑 sanity；
- 未跑 forward；
- 未评估 Test1/Test2。

**tool：**

================ HCRN-v2A-lr README
# HCRN-v2A-lr 改动说明

## 目标

只测试 HCRN-v2 adapter 是否因为学习率过低、gate 被 weight decay 拉回 0 而影响太弱。

## 修改文件

`train_ceph2015.py`

## 具体改动

- 第 70 行：新增 `build_hcrn_optimizer(model, args)`。
- 第 81 行：`hcrn_v2_gates` 和未来可能出现的 `hcrn_v2_coord_gates` 被归入 gate 参数组。
- 第 88-103 行：Adam 分成三组：
- base 参数：`lr=args.lr`，`weight_decay=1e-4`；
- HCRN adapter 参数：`lr=args.lr * args.hcrn_lr_mult`，`weight_decay=0.0`；
- HCRN gate 参数：`lr=args.lr * args.hcrn_gate_lr_mult`，`weight_decay=0.0`。
- 第 106 行：新增 `hcrn_attention_entropy(model)`，记录 uncertain→certain attention 是否接近均匀。
- 第 150 和 154 行：optimizer 创建改为 `build_hcrn_optimizer(model, args)`。
- 第 171-175 行：训练日志打印 HCRN optimizer multiplier。
- 第 344-346 行：每个 epoch 打印 attention entropy。
- 第 415-418 行：新增参数：
- `--hcrn_lr_mult`，默认 `5.0`；
- `--hcrn_gate_lr_mult`，默认 `10.0`。

## 未改动

- 不改 HCRN-v2 网络结构；
- 不改 loss；
- 不改 checkpoint guard；
- 不改 eval 脚本。

## 预期使用

```bash
python train_ceph2015.py \
--hcrn_v2 \
--hcrn_lr_mult 5 \
--hcrn_gate_lr_mult 10 \
--target_mode observer_mixed_nll \
--observer_alpha 0.50
```

================ HCRN-v2B-group-loss README
# HCRN-v2B-group-loss 改动说明

## 目标

在 v2A-lr 的基础上，验证 uncertain group 是否需要更强双标注监督和更高 loss 权重。

## 修改文件

`train_ceph2015.py`

## 具体改动

- 继承 v2A-lr 的 optimizer 分组和 attention entropy 日志。
- 第 70 行：新增 `observer_aware_rle_grouped(...)`。
- 第 91-113 行：certain group 使用 `alpha_certain`，uncertain group 使用 `alpha_uncertain`，并用 `uncertain_weight` 提高 uncertain loss 权重。
- 第 219-227 行：训练日志打印 group loss 参数。
- 第 269-325 行：当 `args.hcrn_v2 and args.hcrn_group_loss` 时，对 `inint_loss_` 和四层 refinement loss 全部使用 grouped loss。
- 第 530-538 行：新增参数：
- `--hcrn_group_loss`
- `--hcrn_alpha_certain`，默认 `0.3`
- `--hcrn_alpha_uncertain`，默认 `0.7`
- `--hcrn_uncertain_weight`，默认 `1.5`

## 未改动

- 不改 HCRN-v2 网络结构；
- 不改 eval 脚本；
- 不把 group loss 和 relative geometry / coord residual 混合。

## 预期使用

```bash
python train_ceph2015.py \
--hcrn_v2 \
--hcrn_lr_mult 5 \
--hcrn_gate_lr_mult 10 \
--hcrn_group_loss \
--hcrn_alpha_certain 0.3 \
--hcrn_alpha_uncertain 0.7 \
--hcrn_uncertain_weight 1.5 \
--target_mode observer_mixed_nll \
--observer_alpha 0.50
```

================ HCRN-v2C-relative-geo README
# HCRN-v2C-relative-geo 改动说明

## 目标

在 v2A-lr 的基础上，让 HCRN-v2 directed adapter 显式看到 uncertain 点相对 certain 点的几何关系。

## 修改文件

- `train_ceph2015.py`
- `ceph_reg_refine_net.py`

## 具体改动

`train_ceph2015.py`

- 继承 v2A-lr 的 optimizer 分组和 attention entropy 日志。

`ceph_reg_refine_net.py`

- 第 500 行：新增 `self.hcrn_v2_rel_pe`，每层一个 `Linear(5,C) -> GELU -> Linear(C,C)`。
- 第 590 行：构造相对几何输入：
- `rel = coords_uncertain - coords_certain`
- `rel.abs()`
- `dist = ||rel||`
- 拼成 `[dx, dy, |dx|, |dy|, dist]`
- 第 591-592 行：用 attention 权重加权聚合 relation feature。
- 第 594 行：`update_proj` 输入从 `cond` 改成 `cond + rel_cond`。

## 未改动

- 不改 loss；
- 不加 uncertain-specific coord residual；
- 不改 checkpoint guard；
- HCRN gate 仍然 zero-init，初始仍等价基线。

## 预期使用

```bash
python train_ceph2015.py \
--hcrn_v2 \
--hcrn_lr_mult 5 \
--hcrn_gate_lr_mult 10 \
--target_mode observer_mixed_nll \
--observer_alpha 0.50
```

================ HCRN-v2D-uncertain-coord-residual README
# HCRN-v2D-uncertain-coord-residual 改动说明

## 目标

在 v2A-lr 的基础上，验证 HCRN adapter 的 token 更新是否被共享 coordinate head 稀释。该分支给 uncertain 点增加一个专属坐标残差头。

## 修改文件

- `train_ceph2015.py`
- `ceph_reg_refine_net.py`

## 具体改动

`ceph_reg_refine_net.py`

- 第 500 行：新增 `self.hcrn_v2_uncertain_coord_heads`，每层一个 `Linear(C,C) -> GELU -> Linear(C,2)`。
- 第 510 行：新增 `self.hcrn_v2_coord_gates`，zero-init。
- 第 669-674 行：在共享 `fc_coord_branches[i]` 输出后，只对 uncertain 点加专属残差：
- `delta_u = hcrn_v2_uncertain_coord_heads[i](lm_uncertain)`
- `coord_gate = 0.05 * tanh(hcrn_v2_coord_gates[i])`
- `tmp_u = tmp_u + coord_gate * delta_u`

`train_ceph2015.py`

- 继承 v2A-lr 的 optimizer 分组。
- 第 81 行：`hcrn_v2_coord_gates` 被归入 gate 参数组，因此无 weight decay 且使用 gate LR multiplier。
- 第 344-352 行：训练日志额外打印 `HCRN-v2 coord_gates raw/bounded`。

## 未改动

- 不改 loss；
- 不加 relative geometry；
- 不改 checkpoint guard；
- directed adapter gate 和 coord residual gate 都 zero-init。

## 预期使用

```bash
python train_ceph2015.py \
--hcrn_v2 \
--hcrn_lr_mult 5 \
--hcrn_gate_lr_mult 10 \
--target_mode observer_mixed_nll \
--observer_alpha 0.50
```

50
51	def observer_aware_rle(loss_fn, output, mean_target, observer_target, target_mode, alpha):
52	    """Mean-anchored dual-annotation RLE for DuoAnno second-model control."""
53	    mean_loss = loss_fn(output, mean_target)
54	    if target_mode == "mean":
55	        return mean_loss
56	    if observer_target is None:
57	        raise ValueError("observer_target is required for observer-aware target modes")
58
59	    observer_loss = 0.5 * (
60	        loss_fn(output, observer_target[:, 0]) +
61	        loss_fn(output, observer_target[:, 1])
62	    )
63	    if target_mode == "observer_avg_nll":
64	        return observer_loss
65	    if target_mode == "observer_mixed_nll":
66	        return (1.0 - alpha) * mean_loss + alpha * observer_loss
67	    raise ValueError(f"Unsupported target_mode: {target_mode}")
68
69
70	def build_hcrn_optimizer(model, args):
71	    """Use stronger LR for HCRN-v2 adapter and no weight decay on adapter/gates."""
72	    if not args.hcrn_v2:
73	        return optim.Adam(model.parameters(), lr=args.lr, weight_decay=1e-4)
74
75	    base_params = []
76	    hcrn_adapter_params = []
77	    hcrn_gate_params = []
78	    for name, param in model.named_parameters():
79	        if not param.requires_grad:
80	            continue
81	        if name in {"hcrn_v2_gates", "hcrn_v2_coord_gates"}:
82	            hcrn_gate_params.append(param)
83	        elif name.startswith("hcrn_v2_"):
84	            hcrn_adapter_params.append(param)
85	        else:
86	            base_params.append(param)
87
88	    param_groups = [
89	        {"params": base_params, "lr": args.lr, "weight_decay": 1e-4, "name": "base"},
90	        {
91	            "params": hcrn_adapter_params,
92	            "lr": args.lr * args.hcrn_lr_mult,
93	            "weight_decay": 0.0,
94	            "name": "hcrn_adapter",
95	        },
96	        {
97	            "params": hcrn_gate_params,
98	            "lr": args.lr * args.hcrn_gate_lr_mult,
99	            "weight_decay": 0.0,
100	            "name": "hcrn_gate",
101	        },
102	    ]
103	    return optim.Adam(param_groups)
104
105
106	def hcrn_attention_entropy(model):
107	    """Return per-layer entropy of uncertain->certain attention, normalized by log(Nc)."""
108	    if not getattr(model, "hcrn_v2", False) or model.hcrn_v2_last_attn is None:
109	        return None
110	    values = []
111	    for attn in model.hcrn_v2_last_attn:
112	        if attn is None:
113	            values.append(float("nan"))
114	            continue
115	        prob = attn.detach().float().clamp_min(1e-12)
116	        entropy = -(prob * prob.log()).sum(dim=-1).mean()
117	        norm = entropy / math.log(prob.shape[-1])
118	        values.append(float(norm.cpu().item()))
119	    return values
120

50
51	def observer_aware_rle(loss_fn, output, mean_target, observer_target, target_mode, alpha):
52	    """Mean-anchored dual-annotation RLE for DuoAnno second-model control."""
53	    mean_loss = loss_fn(output, mean_target)
54	    if target_mode == "mean":
55	        return mean_loss
56	    if observer_target is None:
57	        raise ValueError("observer_target is required for observer-aware target modes")
58
59	    observer_loss = 0.5 * (
60	        loss_fn(output, observer_target[:, 0]) +
61	        loss_fn(output, observer_target[:, 1])
62	    )
63	    if target_mode == "observer_avg_nll":
64	        return observer_loss
65	    if target_mode == "observer_mixed_nll":
66	        return (1.0 - alpha) * mean_loss + alpha * observer_loss
67	    raise ValueError(f"Unsupported target_mode: {target_mode}")
68
69
70	def observer_aware_rle_grouped(
71	    loss_fn,
72	    output,
73	    mean_target,
74	    observer_target,
75	    certain_idx,
76	    uncertain_idx,
77	    alpha_certain=0.3,
78	    alpha_uncertain=0.7,
79	    uncertain_weight=1.5,
80	):
81	    """Apply stronger dual-annotation supervision to high-disagreement landmarks."""
82	    if observer_target is None:
83	        raise ValueError("observer_target is required for HCRN grouped loss")
84
85	    out_c = output[:, certain_idx]
86	    out_u = output[:, uncertain_idx]
87	    mean_c = mean_target[:, certain_idx]
88	    mean_u = mean_target[:, uncertain_idx]
89	    obs_c = observer_target[:, :, certain_idx]
90	    obs_u = observer_target[:, :, uncertain_idx]
91
92	    loss_c = observer_aware_rle(
93	        loss_fn,
94	        out_c,
95	        mean_c,
96	        obs_c,
97	        target_mode="observer_mixed_nll",
98	        alpha=alpha_certain,
99	    )
100	    loss_u = observer_aware_rle(
101	        loss_fn,
102	        out_u,
103	        mean_u,
104	        obs_u,
105	        target_mode="observer_mixed_nll",
106	        alpha=alpha_uncertain,
107	    )
108
109	    nc = float(len(certain_idx))
110	    nu = float(len(uncertain_idx))
111	    return (nc * loss_c + uncertain_weight * nu * loss_u) / (
112	        nc + uncertain_weight * nu
113	    )
114
115

500	                        help='random seed (default: 1)')

521	                        help='Limit training samples for smoke/overfit checks; 0 means full training set')
522	    parser.add_argument('--hcrn_v2', action='store_true',
523	                        help='Enable HCRN-v2 in-DELR directed coordinate conditioning')
524	    parser.add_argument('--hcrn_group_path', type=str, default='',
525	                        help='Optional train-only HCRN group JSON path')
526	    parser.add_argument('--hcrn_lr_mult', type=float, default=5.0,
527	                        help='Learning-rate multiplier for HCRN-v2 adapter parameters')
528	    parser.add_argument('--hcrn_gate_lr_mult', type=float, default=10.0,
529	                        help='Learning-rate multiplier for HCRN-v2 gate parameters')
530	    parser.add_argument('--hcrn_group_loss', action='store_true',
531	                        help='Use group-specific DuoAnno loss for HCRN certain/uncertain landmarks')
532	    parser.add_argument('--hcrn_alpha_certain', type=float, default=0.3,
533	                        help='Observer mixture alpha for low-disagreement landmarks')
534	    parser.add_argument('--hcrn_alpha_uncertain', type=float, default=0.7,
535	                        help='Observer mixture alpha for high-disagreement landmarks')
536	    parser.add_argument('--hcrn_uncertain_weight', type=float, default=1.5,
537	                        help='Extra loss weight for high-disagreement landmarks')
538	    args = parser.parse_args()
539
540	    os.environ['DELR_HCRN_V2'] = '1' if args.hcrn_v2 else '0'
541	    if args.hcrn_group_path:
542	        os.environ['DELR_HCRN_GROUP_PATH'] = args.hcrn_group_path
543	    else:
544	        os.environ.pop('DELR_HCRN_GROUP_PATH', None)

522	    def initialize_weights(self):
523	        # initialization
524	        # initialize (and freeze) pos_embed by sin-cos embedding
525	        pos_embed = get_2d_sincos_pos_embed(self.pos_embed.shape[-1], self.sizem, cls_token=False)
526	        self.pos_embed.data.copy_(torch.from_numpy(pos_embed).float().unsqueeze(0))
527
528	        pos_embedly1 = get_2d_sincos_pos_embed(self.pos_embedly1.shape[-1], self.sizem*8, cls_token=False)
529	        pos_embedly1 = pos_embedly1.reshape(self.sizem[0]*8, self.sizem[1]*8, 64)
530	        self.pos_embedly1.data.copy_(torch.from_numpy(pos_embedly1).float().unsqueeze(0))
531
532
533	        pos_embedly2 = get_2d_sincos_pos_embed(self.pos_embedly2.shape[-1], self.sizem*4, cls_token=False)
534	        pos_embedly2 = pos_embedly2.reshape(self.sizem[0] * 4, self.sizem[1] * 4, 128)
535	        self.pos_embedly2.data.copy_(torch.from_numpy(pos_embedly2).float().unsqueeze(0))
536
537	        pos_embedly3 = get_2d_sincos_pos_embed(self.pos_embedly3.shape[-1], self.sizem*2, cls_token=False)
538	        pos_embedly3 = pos_embedly3.reshape(self.sizem[0] * 2, self.sizem[1] * 2, 256)
539	        self.pos_embedly3.data.copy_(torch.from_numpy(pos_embedly3).float().unsqueeze(0))
540
541
542	        device = torch.device("cuda")
543	        pos_embed1 = PositionalEncoding(self.encoder_embed.shape[1], self.encoder_embed.shape[2], device)
544	        self.encoder_embed.data.copy_(pos_embed1.float().unsqueeze(0))
545
546	    def _get_clones(self, module, N):
547	        return nn.ModuleList([copy.deepcopy(module) for i in range(N)])
548
549	    def _hcrn_v2_directed_conditioning(self, lm_tokens, reference_points, layer_idx):
550	        """Condition uncertain landmark tokens on certain tokens plus explicit coords."""
551	        if not self.hcrn_v2:
552	            return lm_tokens
553
554	        certain_idx = self.hcrn_v2_certain_idx.to(lm_tokens.device)
555	        uncertain_idx = self.hcrn_v2_uncertain_idx.to(lm_tokens.device)
556
557	        lm_certain = torch.index_select(lm_tokens, 1, certain_idx)
558	        lm_uncertain = torch.index_select(lm_tokens, 1, uncertain_idx)
559
560	        coords = reference_points.detach().clamp(0, 1)
561	        coords_certain = torch.index_select(coords, 1, certain_idx).to(lm_tokens.dtype)
562	        coords_uncertain = torch.index_select(coords, 1, uncertain_idx).to(lm_tokens.dtype)
563
564	        certain_kv = lm_certain + self.hcrn_v2_coord_pe(coords_certain)
565	        uncertain_q = lm_uncertain + self.hcrn_v2_coord_pe(coords_uncertain)
566	        certain_kv = self.hcrn_v2_kv_norms[layer_idx](certain_kv)
567	        uncertain_q = self.hcrn_v2_q_norms[layer_idx](uncertain_q)
568
569	        cond, attn = self.hcrn_v2_cross_attn[layer_idx](
570	            query=uncertain_q,
571	            key=certain_kv,
572	            value=certain_kv,
573	            need_weights=True,
574	            average_attn_weights=True,
575	        )
576	        if self.hcrn_v2_last_attn is None:
577	            self.hcrn_v2_last_attn = [None for _ in range(self.NLayer)]
578	        self.hcrn_v2_last_attn[layer_idx] = attn.detach()
579
580	        update = self.hcrn_v2_update_proj[layer_idx](cond)
581	        gate = 0.1 * torch.tanh(self.hcrn_v2_gates[layer_idx]).to(lm_tokens.dtype)
582	        lm_uncertain = lm_uncertain + gate * update
583
584	        return lm_tokens.index_copy(1, uncertain_idx, lm_uncertain)
585
586
587	    def _init_weights(self, m):
588	        if isinstance(m, nn.Linear):
589	            # we use xavier_uniform following official JAX ViT:
590	            torch.nn.init.xavier_uniform_(m.weight)
591	            if isinstance(m, nn.Linear) and m.bias is not None:
592	                nn.init.constant_(m.bias, 0)
593	        elif isinstance(m, nn.LayerNorm):
594	            nn.init.constant_(m.bias, 0)
595	            nn.init.constant_(m.weight, 1.0)
596
597	    def forward(self, x):
598	        if self.hcrn_v2:
599	            self.hcrn_v2_last_attn = None
600	        layer1, layer2, layer3, output = self.backone(x)
601	        hotmap = self.out1(output)
602
603	        b, c, h, w = output.shape
604	        pos1 = self.pos_embedly1.expand(b, -1, -1, -1).permute(0, 3, 1, 2)
605	        pos2 = self.pos_embedly2.expand(b, -1, -1, -1).permute(0, 3, 1, 2)
606	        pos3 = self.pos_embedly3.expand(b, -1, -1, -1).permute(0, 3, 1, 2)
607
608	        layer1 = self.bn1(self.conv1(F.interpolate(layer1, (self.sizem[0], self.sizem[1])))).view(b, c, h* w).permute(0, 2, 1)
609	        layer2 = self.bn2(self.conv2(F.interpolate(layer2, (self.sizem[0], self.sizem[1])))).view(b, c, h* w).permute(0, 2, 1)
610	        layer3 = self.bn3(self.conv3(F.interpolate(layer3, (self.sizem[0], self.sizem[1])))).view(b, c, h* w).permute(0, 2, 1)
630	            inc = cpb(inc)
631	            xcs.append(inc)
632	            inc = inc+pos
633	        output1 = self.linear12(F.relu(self.linear11(xcs[-1][:, -self.n_landmarks:, :])))
634	        #################################################################
635
636	        # xc = (x4 + self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1))
637	        xc = (x4 + self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1))*self.wg[0] + layer1*self.wg[1] + layer2*self.wg[2] + layer3*self.wg[3]
638	        # inint_coords = get_proposal_pos_embed(output1[:, :, :2].detach(), num_pos_feats=512, temperature=10000)
639	        output = x4 + self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1)
640	        inint_coords = get_cls_embed(layer1, layer2, layer3, output, output1[:, :, :2].detach(), sizes, self.wcl, self.n_landmarks)
641
642	        encoder_embed = self.encoder_embed.expand(b, -1, -1)  + inint_coords * self.inintv
643	        # pos = torch.cat([self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1),encoder_embed], dim=1)
644	        # pos = torch.cat([self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1) * self.pg[0] + pos1 * self.pg[1] + pos2 * self.pg[2] + pos3 * self.pg[3], encoder_embed], dim=1)
645
646	        hs = []
647	        inter_references = []
648	        xc_ = torch.cat([xc, encoder_embed], dim=1)
649	        reference_points = output1[:, :, :2].detach().clip(0, 1)
650	        init_reference = reference_points
651	        for i, cpb in enumerate(self.transblock):
652	            xc_ = cpb(xc_)
653	            lm_tokens = xc_[:, -self.n_landmarks:, :]
654	            lm_tokens = self._hcrn_v2_directed_conditioning(lm_tokens, reference_points, i)
655	            xc_ = torch.cat([xc_[:, :-self.n_landmarks, :], lm_tokens], dim=1)
656	            tmp = self.fc_coord_branches[i](xc_[:, -self.n_landmarks:, :])
657
658	            new_reference_points = tmp + inverse_sigmoid(reference_points)
659	            new_reference_points = new_reference_points.sigmoid()
660
661	            reference_points = new_reference_points
662
663	            inint_coords = get_cls_embed(layer1, layer2, layer3, output, new_reference_points.detach(), sizes, self.wcl, self.n_landmarks)
664	            # inint_coords = get_proposal_pos_embed(new_reference_points.detach(), num_pos_feats=512, temperature=10000)
665	            encoder_embed = self.encoder_embed.expand(b, -1, -1) + inint_coords * self.inintv
666	            pos = torch.cat([self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1) * self.pg[0] + pos1 * self.pg[1] + pos2 * self.pg[2] + pos3 * self.pg[3], encoder_embed], dim=1)
667	            xc_ = xc_ + pos
668
669	            inter_references.append(reference_points)
670	            hs.append(xc_[:, -self.n_landmarks:, :])
671	        outputs = []
672	        for lvl in range(len(inter_references)):
673	            if lvl == 0:
674	                reference = init_reference
675	            else:
676	                reference = inter_references[lvl - 1]
677	            reference = inverse_sigmoid(reference)
678
679	            tmp = self.fc_coord_branches[lvl](hs[lvl])
680	            tmp = tmp + reference
681
682
683	            outputs_sigma = self.fc_sigma_branches[lvl](hs[lvl])
684
685
686	            outputs_coord = tmp.sigmoid()
687	            delta_coord_output = self.fc_coord_output_branches[lvl](hs[lvl])
688	            outputs_coord = (outputs_coord + delta_coord_output)
689
690	            outputs_coord = torch.cat([outputs_coord, outputs_sigma], dim=-1)
691	            outputs.append(outputs_coord)
692
693	        # output = F.relu(self.linear21(xcs[-1][:, -encoder_embed.shape[1]:, :]))
694	        # output = self.linear22(output)
695
696
697	        return outputs, output1, hotmap

520	                 residual=True,
550	        device = torch.device("cuda")
551	        pos_embed1 = PositionalEncoding(self.encoder_embed.shape[1], self.encoder_embed.shape[2], device)
552	        self.encoder_embed.data.copy_(pos_embed1.float().unsqueeze(0))
553
554	    def _get_clones(self, module, N):
555	        return nn.ModuleList([copy.deepcopy(module) for i in range(N)])
556
557	    def _hcrn_v2_directed_conditioning(self, lm_tokens, reference_points, layer_idx):
558	        """Condition uncertain landmark tokens on certain tokens plus explicit coords."""
559	        if not self.hcrn_v2:
560	            return lm_tokens
561
562	        certain_idx = self.hcrn_v2_certain_idx.to(lm_tokens.device)
563	        uncertain_idx = self.hcrn_v2_uncertain_idx.to(lm_tokens.device)
564
565	        lm_certain = torch.index_select(lm_tokens, 1, certain_idx)
566	        lm_uncertain = torch.index_select(lm_tokens, 1, uncertain_idx)
567
568	        coords = reference_points.detach().clamp(0, 1)
569	        coords_certain = torch.index_select(coords, 1, certain_idx).to(lm_tokens.dtype)
570	        coords_uncertain = torch.index_select(coords, 1, uncertain_idx).to(lm_tokens.dtype)
571
572	        certain_kv = lm_certain + self.hcrn_v2_coord_pe(coords_certain)
573	        uncertain_q = lm_uncertain + self.hcrn_v2_coord_pe(coords_uncertain)
574	        certain_kv = self.hcrn_v2_kv_norms[layer_idx](certain_kv)
575	        uncertain_q = self.hcrn_v2_q_norms[layer_idx](uncertain_q)
576
577	        cond, attn = self.hcrn_v2_cross_attn[layer_idx](
578	            query=uncertain_q,
579	            key=certain_kv,
580	            value=certain_kv,
581	            need_weights=True,
582	            average_attn_weights=True,
583	        )
584	        if self.hcrn_v2_last_attn is None:
585	            self.hcrn_v2_last_attn = [None for _ in range(self.NLayer)]
586	        self.hcrn_v2_last_attn[layer_idx] = attn.detach()
587
588	        rel = coords_uncertain.unsqueeze(2) - coords_certain.unsqueeze(1)
589	        dist = torch.norm(rel, dim=-1, keepdim=True)
590	        rel_input = torch.cat([rel, rel.abs(), dist], dim=-1)
591	        rel_feat = self.hcrn_v2_rel_pe[layer_idx](rel_input)
592	        rel_cond = (attn.to(lm_tokens.dtype).unsqueeze(-1) * rel_feat).sum(dim=2)
593
594	        update = self.hcrn_v2_update_proj[layer_idx](cond + rel_cond)
595	        gate = 0.1 * torch.tanh(self.hcrn_v2_gates[layer_idx]).to(lm_tokens.dtype)
596	        lm_uncertain = lm_uncertain + gate * update
597
598	        return lm_tokens.index_copy(1, uncertain_idx, lm_uncertain)
599
600
601	    def _init_weights(self, m):
602	        if isinstance(m, nn.Linear):
603	            # we use xavier_uniform following official JAX ViT:
604	            torch.nn.init.xavier_uniform_(m.weight)
605	            if isinstance(m, nn.Linear) and m.bias is not None:
606	                nn.init.constant_(m.bias, 0)
607	        elif isinstance(m, nn.LayerNorm):
608	            nn.init.constant_(m.bias, 0)
609	            nn.init.constant_(m.weight, 1.0)
610
640	        pos = torch.cat([self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1), self.encoder_embed.expand(b, -1, -1)], dim=1)
641
642	        xcs = []
643	        for cpb in self.InitBlock:
644	            inc = cpb(inc)
645	            xcs.append(inc)
646	            inc = inc+pos
647	        output1 = self.linear12(F.relu(self.linear11(xcs[-1][:, -self.n_landmarks:, :])))
648	        #################################################################
649
650	        # xc = (x4 + self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1))
651	        xc = (x4 + self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1))*self.wg[0] + layer1*self.wg[1] + layer2*self.wg[2] + layer3*self.wg[3]
652	        # inint_coords = get_proposal_pos_embed(output1[:, :, :2].detach(), num_pos_feats=512, temperature=10000)
653	        output = x4 + self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1)
654	        inint_coords = get_cls_embed(layer1, layer2, layer3, output, output1[:, :, :2].detach(), sizes, self.wcl, self.n_landmarks)
655
656	        encoder_embed = self.encoder_embed.expand(b, -1, -1)  + inint_coords * self.inintv
657	        # pos = torch.cat([self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1),encoder_embed], dim=1)
658	        # pos = torch.cat([self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1) * self.pg[0] + pos1 * self.pg[1] + pos2 * self.pg[2] + pos3 * self.pg[3], encoder_embed], dim=1)
659
660	        hs = []
661	        inter_references = []
662	        xc_ = torch.cat([xc, encoder_embed], dim=1)
663	        reference_points = output1[:, :, :2].detach().clip(0, 1)
664	        init_reference = reference_points
665	        for i, cpb in enumerate(self.transblock):
666	            xc_ = cpb(xc_)
667	            lm_tokens = xc_[:, -self.n_landmarks:, :]
668	            lm_tokens = self._hcrn_v2_directed_conditioning(lm_tokens, reference_points, i)
669	            xc_ = torch.cat([xc_[:, :-self.n_landmarks, :], lm_tokens], dim=1)
670	            tmp = self.fc_coord_branches[i](xc_[:, -self.n_landmarks:, :])
671
672	            new_reference_points = tmp + inverse_sigmoid(reference_points)
673	            new_reference_points = new_reference_points.sigmoid()
674
675	            reference_points = new_reference_points
676
677	            inint_coords = get_cls_embed(layer1, layer2, layer3, output, new_reference_points.detach(), sizes, self.wcl, self.n_landmarks)
678	            # inint_coords = get_proposal_pos_embed(new_reference_points.detach(), num_pos_feats=512, temperature=10000)
679	            encoder_embed = self.encoder_embed.expand(b, -1, -1) + inint_coords * self.inintv
680	            pos = torch.cat([self.pos_embed.expand(b, -1, -1) * self.pg[0] + pos1 * self.pg[1] + pos2 * self.pg[2] + pos3 * self.pg[3], encoder_embed], dim=1)
681	            xc_ = xc_ + pos
682
683	            inter_references.append(reference_points)
684	            hs.append(xc_[:, -self.n_landmarks:, :])
685	        outputs = []
686	        for lvl in range(len(inter_references)):
687	            if lvl == 0:
688	                reference = init_reference
689	            else:
690	                reference = inter_references[lvl - 1]
691	            reference = inverse_sigmoid(reference)
692
693	            tmp = self.fc_coord_branches[lvl](hs[lvl])
694	            tmp = tmp + reference
695
696
697	            outputs_sigma = self.fc_sigma_branches[lvl](hs[lvl])
698
699
700	            outputs_coord = tmp.sigmoid()

591	        lm_uncertain = lm_uncertain + gate * update
592
593	        return lm_tokens.index_copy(1, uncertain_idx, lm_uncertain)

# ------------------------------------------------------------------------------

from __future__ import absolute_import
from __future__ import division
from __future__ import print_function

import os
import math
import logging
import copy
import json
import numpy as np
import torch
import torch.nn as nn
from torch.nn import functional as F
import torch.utils.model_zoo as model_zoo
from functools import partial
from net.reg_loss import RLELoss
from config import  config as cfg

BN_MOMENTUM = 0.1
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class Block(nn.Module):
def __init__(self, dim, num_heads, mlp_ratio=4.0, qkv_bias=True, norm_layer=nn.LayerNorm):
super().__init__()
self.norm1 = norm_layer(dim)
self.attn = nn.MultiheadAttention(dim, num_heads, bias=qkv_bias, batch_first=True)
self.norm2 = norm_layer(dim)
hidden_dim = int(dim * mlp_ratio)
self.mlp = nn.Sequential(
nn.Linear(dim, hidden_dim),
nn.GELU(),
nn.Linear(hidden_dim, dim),
)

def forward(self, x):
attn_input = self.norm1(x)
attn_out, _ = self.attn(attn_input, attn_input, attn_input, need_weights=False)
x = x + attn_out
x = x + self.mlp(self.norm2(x))
return x

def _load_hcrn_v2_groups(num_landmarks):
"""Load train-only disagreement groups for HCRN-v2 directed conditioning."""
default_certain = [11, 10, 8, 0, 6, 7, 1, 16, 13, 14]
default_uncertain = [17, 18, 12, 5, 2, 4, 3, 9, 15]
group_path = os.environ.get("DELR_HCRN_GROUP_PATH", "")

if group_path:
with open(group_path, "r") as f:
data = json.load(f)
certain = (

def _load_hcrn_v2_groups(num_landmarks):
"""Load train-only disagreement groups for HCRN-v2 directed conditioning."""
default_certain = [11, 10, 8, 0, 6, 7, 1, 16, 13, 14]
default_uncertain = [17, 18, 12, 5, 2, 4, 3, 9, 15]
group_path = os.environ.get("DELR_HCRN_GROUP_PATH", "")

if group_path:
with open(group_path, "r") as f:
data = json.load(f)
certain = (
data.get("certain_idx")
or data.get("certain_indices")
or data.get("certain")
)
uncertain = (
data.get("uncertain_idx")
or data.get("uncertain_indices")
or data.get("uncertain")
)
if certain is None or uncertain is None:
raise ValueError(
"HCRN group JSON must contain certain_idx/certain_indices and "
"uncertain_idx/uncertain_indices."
)
else:
certain = default_certain
uncertain = default_uncertain

certain = [int(x) for x in certain]
uncertain = [int(x) for x in uncertain]
merged = sorted(certain + uncertain)
if merged != list(range(num_landmarks)):
raise ValueError(
f"HCRN groups must be a permutation of 0..{num_landmarks - 1}; "
f"got certain={certain}, uncertain={uncertain}"
)
return certain, uncertain, group_path

def PositionalEncoding(max_len, d_model, device):
encoding = torch.zeros(max_len, d_model, device=device)
encoding.requires_grad = False
pos = torch.arange(0, max_len, device=device).float().unsqueeze(dim=1)
div_term = torch.arange(0, d_model, step=2, device=device).float()
div_term = 10000 ** (div_term / d_model)
